# <a name="routing-in-aspnet-core"></a><span data-ttu-id="f01e9-103">ASP.NET Core 中的路由</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-103">Routing in ASP.NET Core</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-104">作者：[Ryan Nowak](https://github.com/rynowak)、[Steve Smith](https://ardalis.com/) 和 [Rick Anderson](https://twitter.com/RickAndMSFT)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-104">By [Ryan Nowak](https://github.com/rynowak), [Steve Smith](https://ardalis.com/), and [Rick Anderson](https://twitter.com/RickAndMSFT)</span></span>

::: moniker range=">= aspnetcore-3.0"

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-105">路由會負責將要求 Uri 對應至端點，並將傳入要求分派至這些端點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-105">Routing is responsible for mapping request URIs to endpoints and dispatching incoming requests to those endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-106">路由定義於應用程式，並在該應用程式啟動時進行設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-106">Routes are defined in the app and configured when the app starts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-107">路由可以選擇性地從要求中所包含的 URL 擷取值，然後這些值就可用於處理要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-107">A route can optionally extract values from the URL contained in the request, and these values can then be used for request processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-108">使用來自應用程式的路由資訊，路由也能夠產生對應至端點的 Url。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-108">Using route information from the app, routing is also able to generate URLs that map to endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-109">許多應用程式不需要新增範本所提供的路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-109">Many apps don't need to add routes beyond what the templates provide.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-110">控制器和 Razor 頁面的 ASP.NET Core 範本會設定路由端點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-110">The ASP.NET Core templates for controllers and Razor pages configure route endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-111">如果您需要新增自訂路由端點，可以在範本產生的路由端點旁設定自訂端點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-111">If you need to add custom route endpoints, the custom endpoints can be configured alongside template generated route endpoints.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-112">本文件涵蓋低階的 ASP.NET Core 路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-112">This document covers low-level ASP.NET Core routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-113">如需 ASP.NET Core MVC 路由的資訊，請參閱 <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-113">For information on ASP.NET Core MVC routing, see <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-114">如需 Razor Pages 中路由慣例的資訊，請參閱 <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-114">For information on routing conventions in Razor Pages, see <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-115">[檢視或下載範例程式碼](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples) \(英文\) ([如何下載](xref:index#how-to-download-a-sample))</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-115">[View or download sample code](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples) ([how to download](xref:index#how-to-download-a-sample))</span></span>

## <a name="routing-basics"></a><span data-ttu-id="f01e9-116">路由的基本概念</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-116">Routing basics</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-117">大部分應用程式都應該選擇基本的描述性路由傳送配置，讓 URL 可讀且有意義。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-117">Most apps should choose a basic and descriptive routing scheme so that URLs are readable and meaningful.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-118">預設慣例路由 `{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}`：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-118">The default conventional route `{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}`:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-119">支援基本的描述性路由配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-119">Supports a basic and descriptive routing scheme.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-120">適合作為 UI 型應用程式的起點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-120">Is a useful starting point for UI-based apps.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-121">在特殊情況下，開發人員通常會使用[屬性路由](xref:mvc/controllers/routing#attribute-routing)或專屬的慣例路由，新增額外的簡潔路由到應用程式的高流量區域 (例如，部落格和電子商務端點)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-121">Developers commonly add additional terse routes to high-traffic areas of an app in specialized situations (for example, blog and ecommerce endpoints) using [attribute routing](xref:mvc/controllers/routing#attribute-routing) or dedicated conventional routes.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-122">Web API 應該使用屬性路由傳送來將應用程式功能模型建構為作業由 HTTP 指令動詞代表的資源集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-122">Web APIs should use attribute routing to model the app's functionality as a set of resources where operations are represented by HTTP verbs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-123">這表示相同邏輯資源上的許多作業 (例如，GET、POST) 都會使用相同的 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-123">This means that many operations (for example, GET, POST) on the same logical resource will use the same URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-124">屬性路由提供仔細設計 API 公用端點配置所需的控制層級。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-124">Attribute routing provides a level of control that's needed to carefully design an API's public endpoint layout.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-125">Razor Pages 應用程式使用預設慣例路由，來提供應用程式 *Pages* 資料夾中的具名資源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-125">Razor Pages apps use default conventional routing to serve named resources in the *Pages* folder of an app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-126">還有其他慣例可讓您自訂 Razor Pages 路由行為。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-126">Additional conventions are available that allow you to customize Razor Pages routing behavior.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-127">如需詳細資訊，請參閱<xref:razor-pages/index>和<xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-127">For more information, see <xref:razor-pages/index> and <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-128">URL 產生支援允許在不需要硬式編碼的 URL 來連結應用程式的情況下開發應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-128">URL generation support allows the app to be developed without hard-coding URLs to link the app together.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-129">這項支援可讓您從基本路由設定開始，並在決定應用程式資源配置之後修改路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-129">This support allows for starting with a basic routing configuration and modifying the routes after the app's resource layout is determined.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-130">路由功能使用「端點」(`Endpoint`) 來表示應用程式中的邏輯端點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-130">Routing uses *endpoints* (`Endpoint`) to represent logical endpoints in an app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-131">端點會定義用來處理要求的一項委派及一個任意中繼資料集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-131">An endpoint defines a delegate to process requests and a collection of arbitrary metadata.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-132">中繼資料是用來根據附加至每個端點的原則和設定來執行跨領域考慮。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-132">The metadata is used to implement cross-cutting concerns based on policies and configuration attached to each endpoint.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-133">路由系統具有下列特性：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-133">The routing system has the following characteristics:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-134">使用路由範本語法以 Token 化路由參數來定義路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-134">Route template syntax is used to define routes with tokenized route parameters.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-135">允許傳統式和屬性式端點組態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-135">Conventional-style and attribute-style endpoint configuration is permitted.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-136"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> 可用來判斷 URL 參數是否包含對指定端點條件約束有效的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-136"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> is used to determine whether a URL parameter contains a valid value for a given endpoint constraint.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-137">應用程式模型 (例如 MVC/Razor Pages) 會註冊其所有端點，這些端點的路由情節實作符合預期。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-137">App models, such as MVC/Razor Pages, register all of their endpoints, which have a predictable implementation of routing scenarios.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-138">路由實作會在中介軟體管線需要時制定路由決策。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-138">The routing implementation makes routing decisions wherever desired in the middleware pipeline.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-139">在路由中介軟體之後出現的中介軟體可以檢查指定要求 URI 的路由中介軟體端點決策。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-139">Middleware that appears after a Routing Middleware can inspect the result of the Routing Middleware's endpoint decision for a given request URI.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-140">您可以針對中介軟體管線中任何位置的應用程式，列舉其中的所有端點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-140">It's possible to enumerate all of the endpoints in the app anywhere in the middleware pipeline.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-141">應用程式可以根據端點資訊使用路由來產生 URL (例如，針對重新導向或連結)，因此避免硬式編碼的 URL，這有助於可維護性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-141">An app can use routing to generate URLs (for example, for redirection or links) based on endpoint information and thus avoid hard-coded URLs, which helps maintainability.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-142">URL 是根據支援任意擴充性的位址所產生：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-142">URL generation is based on addresses, which support arbitrary extensibility:</span></span>

  * <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-143">您可以在任何位置使用[相依性插入 (DI)](xref:fundamentals/dependency-injection) 來解析連結產生器 API (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator>)，以產生 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-143">The Link Generator API (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator>) can be resolved anywhere using [dependency injection (DI)](xref:fundamentals/dependency-injection) to generate URLs.</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-144">如果無法透過 DI 使用連結產生器 API，<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper> 會提供方法來建立 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-144">Where the Link Generator API isn't available via DI, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper> offers methods to build URLs.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-145">端點連結僅限於 MVC/Razor Pages 動作和頁面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-145">Endpoint linking is limited to MVC/Razor Pages actions and pages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-146">未來版本將規劃擴充端點連結功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-146">The expansions of endpoint-linking capabilities is planned for future releases.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-147">路由會透過 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RouterMiddleware> 類別連線到[中介軟體](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index)管線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-147">Routing is connected to the [middleware](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index) pipeline by the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RouterMiddleware> class.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-148">[ASP.NET Core MVC](xref:mvc/overview) 會將路由新增至中介軟體管線，作為其組態的一部分，並處理 MVC 和 Razor Pages 應用程式中的路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-148">[ASP.NET Core MVC](xref:mvc/overview) adds routing to the middleware pipeline as part of its configuration and handles routing in MVC and Razor Pages apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-149">若要了解如何使用路由作為獨立元件，請參閱[使用路由中介軟體](#use-routing-middleware)一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-149">To learn how to use routing as a standalone component, see the [Use Routing Middleware](#use-routing-middleware) section.</span></span>

### <a name="url-matching"></a><span data-ttu-id="f01e9-150">URL 比對</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-150">URL matching</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-151">URL 比對是路由用來將傳入要求分派給「端點」的處理序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-151">URL matching is the process by which routing dispatches an incoming request to an *endpoint*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-152">這個處理序是基於 URL 路徑中的資料，但是可以擴展為考慮要求中的任何資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-152">This process is based on data in the URL path but can be extended to consider any data in the request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-153">分派要求給不同處理常式的能力，是調整應用程式大小和複雜度的關鍵。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-153">The ability to dispatch requests to separate handlers is key to scaling the size and complexity of an app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-154">當路由中介軟體執行時，它會將端點 (`Endpoint`) 和路由值設定為 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpContext> 上的功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-154">When a Routing Middleware executes, it sets an endpoint (`Endpoint`) and route values to a feature on the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpContext>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-155">針對目前的要求：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-155">For the current request:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-156">呼叫 `HttpContext.GetEndpoint` 可取得端點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-156">Calling `HttpContext.GetEndpoint` gets the endpoint.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-157">`HttpRequest.RouteValues` 會取得路由值的集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-157">`HttpRequest.RouteValues` gets the collection of route values.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-158">在路由中介軟體之後執行的中介軟體可以看到端點，並採取動作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-158">Middleware running after the Routing Middleware can see the endpoint and take action.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-159">例如，授權中介軟體可以針對授權原則，查閱端點的中繼資料集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-159">For example, an Authorization Middleware can interrogate the endpoint's metadata collection for an authorization policy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-160">執行要求處理管線中的所有中介軟體之後，會叫用所選端點的委派。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-160">After all of the middleware in the request processing pipeline is executed, the selected endpoint's delegate is invoked.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-161">端點路由中的路由系統負責制定所有分派決策。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-161">The routing system in endpoint routing is responsible for all dispatching decisions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-162">由於中介軟體會根據所選取的端點來套用原則，因此請務必在路由系統內制定可能影響分派或應用安全性原則的任何決策。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-162">Since the middleware applies policies based on the selected endpoint, it's important that any decision that can affect dispatching or the application of security policies is made inside the routing system.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-163">執行端點委派時，會根據到目前為止所執行的要求處理，將 [RouteContext.RouteData](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.RouteData) 的屬性設定為適當的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-163">When the endpoint delegate is executed, the properties of [RouteContext.RouteData](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.RouteData) are set to appropriate values based on the request processing performed thus far.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-164">[RouteData.Values](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Values*) 是「路由值」的字典，而路由值產生自路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-164">[RouteData.Values](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Values*) is a dictionary of *route values* produced from the route.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-165">這些值通常是透過將 URL 語彙基元化來決定，可以用來接受使用者輸入，或在應用程式內做出進一步的分派決策。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-165">These values are usually determined by tokenizing the URL and can be used to accept user input or to make further dispatching decisions inside the app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-166">[RouteData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*) 是其他資料的屬性包，而這些資料與相符路由相關。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-166">[RouteData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*) is a property bag of additional data related to the matched route.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-167">提供了 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*> 來支援與每個路由建立關聯的狀態資料，因此應用程式可以依據符合哪一個路由來制定決策。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-167"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*> are provided to support associating state data with each route so that the app can make decisions based on which route matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-168">這些是開發人員定義的值，**不會**以任何方式影響路由的行為。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-168">These values are developer-defined and do **not** affect the behavior of routing in any way.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-169">此外，儲藏在 [RouteData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*) 中的值可以是任何類型，對比之下，[RouteData.Values](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Values) 則必須可轉換成字串或可從字串轉換。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-169">Additionally, values stashed in [RouteData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*) can be of any type, in contrast to [RouteData.Values](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Values), which must be convertible to and from strings.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-170">[RouteData.Routers](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers) 是成功符合要求的參與路由清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-170">[RouteData.Routers](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers) is a list of the routes that took part in successfully matching the request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-171">路由可以用巢狀方式置於彼此內部。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-171">Routes can be nested inside of one another.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-172"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> 屬性會透過導致產生相符項目的路由邏輯樹狀結構反映路徑。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-172">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> property reflects the path through the logical tree of routes that resulted in a match.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-173">一般而言，<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> 中的第一個項目是路由集合，應該用於產生 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-173">Generally, the first item in <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> is the route collection and should be used for URL generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-174"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> 中的最後一個項目是相符的路由處理常式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-174">The last item in <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> is the route handler that matched.</span></span>

<a name="lg"></a>

### <a name="url-generation-with-linkgenerator"></a><span data-ttu-id="f01e9-175">使用 LinkGenerator 產生 URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-175">URL generation with LinkGenerator</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-176">URL 產生是路由可用來依據一組路由值建立 URL 路徑的處理序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-176">URL generation is the process by which routing can create a URL path based on a set of route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-177">這可讓您在端點和存取它們的 URL 之間建立邏輯分隔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-177">This allows for a logical separation between your endpoints and the URLs that access them.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-178">端點路由包含連結產生器 API (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator>)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-178">Endpoint routing includes the Link Generator API (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator>).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-179"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> 是可從 DI 擷取的單一服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-179"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> is a singleton service that can be retrieved from DI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-180">您可以在執行要求內容外部使用此 API。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-180">The API can be used outside of the context of an executing request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-181">MVC 的 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper> 及依賴 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper> 的情節 (例如[標籤協助程式](xref:mvc/views/tag-helpers/intro)、HTML 協助程式和[動作結果](xref:mvc/controllers/actions)) 均使用連結產生器來提供連結產生功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-181">MVC's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper> and scenarios that rely on <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper>, such as [Tag Helpers](xref:mvc/views/tag-helpers/intro), HTML Helpers, and [Action Results](xref:mvc/controllers/actions), use the link generator to provide link generating capabilities.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-182">連結產生器背後支援的概念為「位址」和「位址配置」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-182">The link generator is backed by the concept of an *address* and *address schemes*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-183">位址配置可讓您判斷應考慮用於連結產生的端點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-183">An address scheme is a way of determining the endpoints that should be considered for link generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-184">例如，MVC/Razor Pages 中許多使用者所熟悉的路由名稱和路由值情節，都會實作為位址配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-184">For example, the route name and route values scenarios many users are familiar with from MVC/Razor Pages are implemented as an address scheme.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-185">連結產生器可以透過下列擴充方法，連結至 MVC/Razor Pages 動作和頁面：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-185">The link generator can link to MVC/Razor Pages actions and pages via the following extension methods:</span></span>

* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.ControllerLinkGeneratorExtensions.GetPathByAction*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.ControllerLinkGeneratorExtensions.GetUriByAction*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.PageLinkGeneratorExtensions.GetPathByPage*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.PageLinkGeneratorExtensions.GetUriByPage*>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-186">這些方法的多載接受包含 `HttpContext` 的引數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-186">An overload of these methods accepts arguments that include the `HttpContext`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-187">這些方法的功能等同於 `Url.Action` 和 `Url.Page`，但提供更多彈性和選項。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-187">These methods are functionally equivalent to `Url.Action` and `Url.Page` but offer additional flexibility and options.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-188">`GetPath*` 方法與 `Url.Action` 和 `Url.Page` 最類似，因為它們會產生包含絕對路徑的 URI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-188">The `GetPath*` methods are most similar to `Url.Action` and `Url.Page` in that they generate a URI containing an absolute path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-189">`GetUri*` 方法一律會產生包含配置和主機的絕對 URI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-189">The `GetUri*` methods always generate an absolute URI containing a scheme and host.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-190">接受 `HttpContext` 的方法會在執行要求的內容中產生 URI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-190">The methods that accept an `HttpContext` generate a URI in the context of the executing request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-191">除非遭到覆寫，否則會使用來自執行要求的環境路由值、URL 基底路徑、配置和主機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-191">The ambient route values, URL base path, scheme, and host from the executing request are used unless overridden.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-192">呼叫 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> 並指定一個位址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-192"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> is called with an address.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-193">執行下列兩個步驟來產生 URI：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-193">Generating a URI occurs in two steps:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-194">將位址繫結至符合該位址的端點清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-194">An address is bound to a list of endpoints that match the address.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-195">評估每個端點的 `RoutePattern`，直到找到符合所提供值的路由模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-195">Each endpoint's `RoutePattern` is evaluated until a route pattern that matches the supplied values is found.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-196">產生的輸出會與提供給連結產生器的其他 URI 組件合併並傳回。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-196">The resulting output is combined with the other URI parts supplied to the link generator and returned.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-197"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> 提供的方法支援適用於任何位址類型的標準連結產生功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-197">The methods provided by <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> support standard link generation capabilities for any type of address.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-198">使用連結產生器的最便利方式是透過執行特定位址類型作業的擴充方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-198">The most convenient way to use the link generator is through extension methods that perform operations for a specific address type.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-199">擴充方法</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-199">Extension Method</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-200">描述</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-200">Description</span></span> |
| ---------------- | ----------- |
| <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator.GetPathByAddress*> | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-201">根據提供的值產生具有絕對路徑的 URI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-201">Generates a URI with an absolute path based on the provided values.</span></span> |
| <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator.GetUriByAddress*> | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-202">根據提供的值產生絕對 URI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-202">Generates an absolute URI based on the provided values.</span></span>             |

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-203">注意呼叫 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> 方法的下列影響：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-203">Pay attention to the following implications of calling <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> methods:</span></span>
>
> * <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-204">使用 `GetUri*` 擴充方法，並注意應用程式組態不會驗證傳入要求的 `Host` 標頭。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-204">Use `GetUri*` extension methods with caution in an app configuration that doesn't validate the `Host` header of incoming requests.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-205">如果傳入要求的 `Host` 標頭未經驗證，則可能將未受信任的要求輸入傳回檢視/頁面 URI 中的用戶端。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-205">If the `Host` header of incoming requests isn't validated, untrusted request input can be sent back to the client in URIs in a view/page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-206">建議所有生產應用程式將其伺服器設定為驗證 `Host` 標頭是否為已知有效值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-206">We recommend that all production apps configure their server to validate the `Host` header against known valid values.</span></span>
>
> * <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-207">使用 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator>，並注意與 `Map` 或 `MapWhen` 搭配使用的中介軟體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-207">Use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> with caution in middleware in combination with `Map` or `MapWhen`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-208">`Map*` 會變更執行要求的基底路徑，這會影響連結產生的輸出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-208">`Map*` changes the base path of the executing request, which affects the output of link generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-209">所有的 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> API 都允許指定基底路徑。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-209">All of the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> APIs allow specifying a base path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-210">請一律指定空白基底路徑來恢復 `Map*` 對連結產生的影響。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-210">Always specify an empty base path to undo `Map*`'s affect on link generation.</span></span>

## <a name="endpoint-routing"></a><span data-ttu-id="f01e9-211">端點路由</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-211">Endpoint routing</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-212">路由端點具有範本、中繼資料，以及服務端點回應的要求委派。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-212">A route endpoint has a template, metadata, and a request delegate that serves the endpoint's response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-213">中繼資料是用來根據附加至每個端點的原則和設定來執行跨領域考慮。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-213">The metadata is used to implement cross-cutting concerns based on policies and configuration attached to each endpoint.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-214">例如，授權中介軟體可以針對[授權原則](xref:security/authorization/policies#applying-policies-to-mvc-controllers)詢問端點的元資料集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-214">For example, an authorization middleware can interrogate the endpoint's metadata collection for an [authorization policy](xref:security/authorization/policies#applying-policies-to-mvc-controllers).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-215">端點路由會使用兩個擴充方法與中介軟體整合：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-215">Endpoint routing integrates with middleware using two extension methods:</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-216">[UseRouting](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseRouting*)會將路由對應新增至中介軟體管線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-216">[UseRouting](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseRouting*) adds route matching to the middleware pipeline.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-217">它必須位於任何路由感知中介軟體之前，例如授權、端點執行等等。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-217">It must come before any route-aware middleware such as authorization, endpoint execution, etc.</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-218">[UseEndpoints](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*)會將端點執行新增至中介軟體管線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-218">[UseEndpoints](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*) adds endpoint execution to the middleware pipeline.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-219">它會執行服務端點回應的要求委派。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-219">It runs the request delegate that serves the endpoint's response.</span></span>
  <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-220">`UseEndpoints` 也是路由端點設定的位置，可由應用程式進行比對和執行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-220">`UseEndpoints` is also where route endpoints are configured that can be matched and executed by the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-221">例如，<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RazorPagesEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRazorPages*>、<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.ControllerEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapControllers*>、<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>和 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPost*>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-221">For example, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RazorPagesEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRazorPages*>, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.ControllerEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapControllers*>, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>, and <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPost*>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-222">應用程式會使用 ASP.NET Core 的 helper 方法來設定其路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-222">Apps use ASP.NET Core's helper methods to configure their routes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-223">ASP.NET Core 架構提供 helper 方法，例如 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RazorPagesEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRazorPages*>、<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.ControllerEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapControllers*> 和 `MapHub<THub>`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-223">ASP.NET Core frameworks provide helper methods like <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RazorPagesEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRazorPages*>, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.ControllerEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapControllers*> and `MapHub<THub>`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-224">另外還有協助程式方法，可用於設定您自己的自訂路由端點： <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>、<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPost*>和[MapVerb](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-224">There are also helper methods for configuring your own custom route endpoints: <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPost*>, and [MapVerb](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions).</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-225">端點路由也支援應用程式啟動後變更的端點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-225">Endpoint routing also supports endpoints changing after an application has started up.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-226">若要在您的應用程式或 ASP.NET Core 架構中支援這項功能，必須建立並註冊自訂 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.EndpointDataSource>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-226">To support this in your app or ASP.NET Core framework, a custom <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.EndpointDataSource> must be created and registered.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-227">這是一項先進的功能，通常不需要。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-227">This is an advanced feature, and usually not needed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-228">端點通常會在啟動時設定，而且在應用程式的存留期為靜態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-228">Endpoints are typically configured at startup and are static for the lifetime of the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-229">在啟動時從檔案或資料庫載入路由設定並非動態的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-229">Loading route configuration from a file or database at startup is not dynamic.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-230">下列程式碼顯示端點路由的基本範例：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-230">The following code shows a basic example of endpoint routing:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/3.x/Startup.cs?name=snippet)]

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-231">如需端點路由的詳細資訊，請參閱本檔中的[URL](#url-matching)比對。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-231">See [URL matching](#url-matching) in this document for more information on endpoint routing.</span></span>

## <a name="endpoint-routing-differences-from-earlier-versions-of-routing"></a><span data-ttu-id="f01e9-232">端點路由與舊版路由的差異</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-232">Endpoint routing differences from earlier versions of routing</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-233">端點路由和之前的路由版本之間存在一些差異，早于 ASP.NET Core 2.2：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-233">A few differences exist between endpoint routing and versions of routing earlier than in ASP.NET Core 2.2:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-234">端點路由系統不支援以 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter> 為基礎的擴充性，包括從 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> 繼承。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-234">The endpoint routing system doesn't support <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>-based extensibility, including inheriting from <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-235">端點路由不支援 [WebApiCompatShim](https://www.nuget.org/packages/Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.WebApiCompatShim)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-235">Endpoint routing doesn't support [WebApiCompatShim](https://www.nuget.org/packages/Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.WebApiCompatShim).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-236">請使用 2.1 [相容性版本](xref:mvc/compatibility-version) (`.SetCompatibilityVersion(CompatibilityVersion.Version_2_1)`) 以繼續使用相容性填充碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-236">Use the 2.1 [compatibility version](xref:mvc/compatibility-version) (`.SetCompatibilityVersion(CompatibilityVersion.Version_2_1)`) to continue using the compatibility shim.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-237">端點路由與使用傳統路由時所產生 URI 大小寫的行為不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-237">Endpoint Routing has different behavior for the casing of generated URIs when using conventional routes.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-238">請考慮下列預設路由範本：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-238">Consider the following default route template:</span></span>

  ```csharp
  app.UseMvc(routes =>
  {
      routes.MapRoute("default", "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
  });
  ```

  <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-239">假設您使用下列路由來產生動作連結：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-239">Suppose you generate a link to an action using the following route:</span></span>

  ```csharp
  var link = Url.Action("ReadPost", "blog", new { id = 17, });
  ```

  <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-240">使用以 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter> 為基礎的路由，此程式碼會產生 `/blog/ReadPost/17` 的 URI，其遵守所提供路由值的大小寫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-240">With <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>-based routing, this code generates a URI of `/blog/ReadPost/17`, which respects the casing of the provided route value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-241">ASP.NET Core 2.2 或更新版本中的端點路由會產生 `/Blog/ReadPost/17` ("Blog" 為大寫)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-241">Endpoint routing in ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later produces `/Blog/ReadPost/17` ("Blog" is capitalized).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-242">端點路由提供 `IOutboundParameterTransformer` 介面，可用來全域自訂此行為，或為對應 URL 套用不同的慣例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-242">Endpoint routing provides the `IOutboundParameterTransformer` interface that can be used to customize this behavior globally or to apply different conventions for mapping URLs.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-243">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[參數轉換器參考](#parameter-transformer-reference)一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-243">For more information, see the [Parameter transformer reference](#parameter-transformer-reference) section.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-244">當嘗試連結至不存在的控制器/動作或頁面時，MVC/Razor Pages 所使用的連結產生與傳統路由的行為不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-244">Link Generation used by MVC/Razor Pages with conventional routes behaves differently when attempting to link to an controller/action or page that doesn't exist.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-245">請考慮下列預設路由範本：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-245">Consider the following default route template:</span></span>

  ```csharp
  app.UseMvc(routes =>
  {
      routes.MapRoute("default", "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
  });
  ```

  <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-246">假設您使用預設範本和下列程式碼來產生動作連結：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-246">Suppose you generate a link to an action using the default template with the following:</span></span>

  ```csharp
  var link = Url.Action("ReadPost", "Blog", new { id = 17, });
  ```

  <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-247">使用以 `IRouter` 為基礎的路由，結果一律為 `/Blog/ReadPost/17`，即使 `BlogController` 不存在或沒有 `ReadPost` 動作方法也一樣。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-247">With `IRouter`-based routing, the result is always `/Blog/ReadPost/17`, even if the `BlogController` doesn't exist or doesn't have a `ReadPost` action method.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-248">如預期，如果動作方法存在，則 ASP.NET Core 2.2 或更新版本中的端點路由會產生 `/Blog/ReadPost/17`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-248">As expected, endpoint routing in ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later produces `/Blog/ReadPost/17` if the action method exists.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-249">不過，如果動作不存在，則端點路由會產生空字串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-249">*However, endpoint routing produces an empty string if the action doesn't exist.*</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-250">就概念而言，如果動作不存在，則端點路由不會假設端點存在。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-250">Conceptually, endpoint routing doesn't assume that the endpoint exists if the action doesn't exist.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-251">連結產生「環境值失效演算法」在搭配端點路由使用時會有不同的行為。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-251">The link generation *ambient value invalidation algorithm* behaves differently when used with endpoint routing.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-252">「環境值失效」是一種演算法，會從目前執行的要求 (環境值) 決定可用於連結產生作業的路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-252">*Ambient value invalidation* is the algorithm that decides which route values from the currently executing request (the ambient values) can be used in link generation operations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-253">傳統路由一律會在連結至其他動作時，使額外的路由值失效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-253">Conventional routing always invalidated extra route values when linking to a different action.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-254">在 ASP.NET Core 2.2 版以前，屬性路由沒有此行為。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-254">Attribute routing didn't have this behavior prior to the release of ASP.NET Core 2.2.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-255">在舊版的 ASP.NET Core 中，連結至使用相同路由參數名稱的其他動作會導致連結產生錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-255">In earlier versions of ASP.NET Core, links to another action that use the same route parameter names resulted in link generation errors.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-256">在 ASP.NET Core 2.2 或更新版本中，這兩種路由形式都會在連結至其他動作時使值失效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-256">In ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later, both forms of routing invalidate values when linking to another action.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-257">請考慮 ASP.NET Core 2.1 或更舊版本中的下列範例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-257">Consider the following example in ASP.NET Core 2.1 or earlier.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-258">連結至其他動作 (或其他頁面) 時，路由值可能會不適當地重複使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-258">When linking to another action (or another page), route values can be reused in undesirable ways.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-259">在 */Pages/Store/Product.cshtml* 中：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-259">In */Pages/Store/Product.cshtml*:</span></span>

  ```cshtml
  @page "{id}"
  @Url.Page("/Login")
  ```

  <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-260">在 */Pages/Login.cshtml* 中：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-260">In */Pages/Login.cshtml*:</span></span>

  ```cshtml
  @page "{id?}"
  ```

  <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-261">如果 URI 在 ASP.NET Core 2.1 或更舊版本中為 `/Store/Product/18`，則 `@Url.Page("/Login")` 在 Store/Info 頁面中產生的連結為 `/Login/18`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-261">If the URI is `/Store/Product/18` in ASP.NET Core 2.1 or earlier, the link generated on the Store/Info page by `@Url.Page("/Login")` is `/Login/18`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-262">這會重複使用 `id` 值 18，即使連結目的地是完全不同的應用程式組件也一樣。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-262">The `id` value of 18 is reused, even though the link destination is different part of the app entirely.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-263">`/Login` 頁面內容中的 `id` 路由值可能是使用者識別碼值，而不是市集產品識別碼值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-263">The `id` route value in the context of the `/Login` page is probably a user ID value, not a store product ID value.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-264">在 ASP.NET Core 2.2 或更新版本中的端點路由中，結果為 `/Login`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-264">In endpoint routing with ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later, the result is `/Login`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-265">當連結的目的地是不同的動作或頁面時，不會重複使用環境值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-265">Ambient values aren't reused when the linked destination is a different action or page.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-266">往返路由參數語法：使用雙星號 (`**`) catch-all 參數語法時，斜線不會經過編碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-266">Round-tripping route parameter syntax: Forward slashes aren't encoded when using a double-asterisk (`**`) catch-all parameter syntax.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-267">在連結產生期間，除了斜線，路由系統還會對雙星號 (`**`) catch-all 參數 (例如 `{**myparametername}`) 中擷取的值進行編碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-267">During link generation, the routing system encodes the value captured in a double-asterisk (`**`) catch-all parameter (for example, `{**myparametername}`) except the forward slashes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-268">ASP.NET Core 2.2 或更新版本中以 `IRouter` 為基礎的路由支援雙星號 catch-all。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-268">The double-asterisk catch-all is supported with `IRouter`-based routing in ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-269">舊版 ASP.NET Core 中的單一星號 catch-all (`{*myparametername}`) 參數語法仍會受到支援，而且斜線會經過編碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-269">The single asterisk catch-all parameter syntax in prior versions of ASP.NET Core (`{*myparametername}`) remains supported, and forward slashes are encoded.</span></span>

  | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-270">路由</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-270">Route</span></span>              | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-271">以下列項目產生的連結：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-271">Link generated with</span></span><br>`Url.Action(new { category = "admin/products" })`&hellip; |
  | ------------------ | --------------------------------------------------------------------- |
  | `/search/{*page}`  | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-272">`/search/admin%2Fproducts` (斜線會經過編碼)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-272">`/search/admin%2Fproducts` (the forward slash is encoded)</span></span>             |
  | `/search/{**page}` | `/search/admin/products`                                              |

### <a name="middleware-example"></a><span data-ttu-id="f01e9-273">中介軟體範例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-273">Middleware example</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-274">在下列範例中，中介軟體使用 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> API 建立列出市集產品的動作方法連結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-274">In the following example, a middleware uses the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> API to create link to an action method that lists store products.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-275">應用程式中的任何類別都可以使用連結產生器，方法是將它插入類別並呼叫 `GenerateLink`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-275">Using the link generator by injecting it into a class and calling `GenerateLink` is available to any class in an app.</span></span>

```csharp
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing;

public class ProductsLinkMiddleware
{
    private readonly LinkGenerator _linkGenerator;

    public ProductsLinkMiddleware(RequestDelegate next, LinkGenerator linkGenerator)
    {
        _linkGenerator = linkGenerator;
    }

    public async Task InvokeAsync(HttpContext httpContext)
    {
        var url = _linkGenerator.GetPathByAction("ListProducts", "Store");

        httpContext.Response.ContentType = "text/plain";

        await httpContext.Response.WriteAsync($"Go to {url} to see our products.");
    }
}
```

### <a name="create-routes"></a><span data-ttu-id="f01e9-276">建立路由</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-276">Create routes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-277">大部分的應用程式會藉由呼叫 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> 或其中一個 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteBuilder> 上定義的類似擴充方法來定建立路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-277">Most apps create routes by calling <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> or one of the similar extension methods defined on <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteBuilder>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-278">任何 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteBuilder> 擴充方法都會建立 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> 的執行個體，並將它新增至路由集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-278">Any of the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteBuilder> extension methods create an instance of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> and add it to the route collection.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-279"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> 不接受路由處理常式參數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-279"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> doesn't accept a route handler parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-280"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> 只會新增 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder.DefaultHandler*> 所處理的路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-280"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> only adds routes that are handled by the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder.DefaultHandler*>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-281">若要深入了解 MVC 中的路由功能，請參閱 <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-281">To learn more about routing in MVC, see <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-282">下列程式碼範例是典型 ASP.NET Core MVC 路由定義所使用的 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> 呼叫範例：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-282">The following code example is an example of a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> call used by a typical ASP.NET Core MVC route definition:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-283">此範本會比對 URL 路徑，並擷取路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-283">This template matches a URL path and extracts the route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-284">例如，路徑 `/Products/Details/17` 會產生下列路由值：`{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 17 }`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-284">For example, the path `/Products/Details/17` generates the following route values: `{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 17 }`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-285">路由值是透過將 URL 路徑分割成區段，並比對每個區段與路由範本中的「路由參數」名稱來判定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-285">Route values are determined by splitting the URL path into segments and matching each segment with the *route parameter* name in the route template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-286">路由參數為具名。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-286">Route parameters are named.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-287">參數是透過以括弧 `{ ... }` 括住參數名稱來定義。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-287">The parameters defined by enclosing the parameter name in braces `{ ... }`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-288">上述範本也可以比對 URL 路徑 `/` 並產生值 `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-288">The preceding template could also match the URL path `/` and produce the values `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-289">發生這種情況是因為 `{controller}` 和 `{action}` 路由參數有預設值，而 `id` 路由參數為選擇性參數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-289">This occurs because the `{controller}` and `{action}` route parameters have default values and the `id` route parameter is optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-290">路由參數名稱之後緊接著值的等號 (`=`) 會定義參數預設值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-290">An equals sign (`=`) followed by a value after the route parameter name defines a default value for the parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-291">路由參數名稱之後的問號 (`?`) 會定義選擇性參數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-291">A question mark (`?`) after the route parameter name defines an optional parameter.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-292">在路由相符時，具有預設值的路由參數一定會產生路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-292">Route parameters with a default value *always* produce a route value when the route matches.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-293">如果沒有任何對應的 URL 路徑區段，選擇性參數不會產生路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-293">Optional parameters don't produce a route value if there was no corresponding URL path segment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-294">如需路由範本情節和語法的詳細描述，請參閱[路由範本參考](#route-template-reference)一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-294">See the [Route template reference](#route-template-reference) section for a thorough description of route template scenarios and syntax.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-295">在下列範例中，路由參數定義 `{id:int}` 會定義 `id` 路由參數的[路由條件約束](#route-constraint-reference)：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-295">In the following example, the route parameter definition `{id:int}` defines a [route constraint](#route-constraint-reference) for the `id` route parameter:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id:int}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-296">此範本會符合 `/Products/Details/17` 等 URL 路徑，但不符合 `/Products/Details/Apples`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-296">This template matches a URL path like `/Products/Details/17` but not `/Products/Details/Apples`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-297">路由條件約束會實作 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>，並檢查路由值以進行驗證。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-297">Route constraints implement <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> and inspect route values to verify them.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-298">在此範例中，路由值 `id` 必須可以轉換為整數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-298">In this example, the route value `id` must be convertible to an integer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-299">如需架構所提供之路由條件約束的說明，請參閱[路由條件約束參考](#route-constraint-reference)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-299">See [route-constraint-reference](#route-constraint-reference) for an explanation of route constraints provided by the framework.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-300"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> 的其他多載接受 `constraints`、`dataTokens` 和 `defaults` 的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-300">Additional overloads of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> accept values for `constraints`, `dataTokens`, and `defaults`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-301">這些參數通常是用來傳遞匿名類型的物件，其中匿名類型的屬性名稱符合路由參數名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-301">The typical usage of these parameters is to pass an anonymously typed object, where the property names of the anonymous type match route parameter names.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-302">下列 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> 範例會建立對等的路由：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-302">The following <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> examples create equivalent routes:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default_route",
    template: "{controller}/{action}/{id?}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Home", action = "Index" });

routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default_route",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
```

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-303">對於簡單的路由而言，定義條件約束和預設的內嵌語法可能很方便。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-303">The inline syntax for defining constraints and defaults can be convenient for simple routes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-304">不過，內嵌語法不支援某些情節 (例如資料語彙基元)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-304">However, there are scenarios, such as data tokens, that aren't supported by inline syntax.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-305">下列範例將示範一些其他情節：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-305">The following example demonstrates a few additional scenarios:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "blog",
    template: "Blog/{**article}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Blog", action = "ReadArticle" });
```

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-306">上述範本會比對 `/Blog/All-About-Routing/Introduction` 等 URL 路徑，並擷取值 `{ controller = Blog, action = ReadArticle, article = All-About-Routing/Introduction }`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-306">The preceding template matches a URL path like `/Blog/All-About-Routing/Introduction` and extracts the values `{ controller = Blog, action = ReadArticle, article = All-About-Routing/Introduction }`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-307">即使範本中沒有任何對應的路由參數，路由也會產生 `controller` 和 `action` 的預設路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-307">The default route values for `controller` and `action` are produced by the route even though there are no corresponding route parameters in the template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-308">預設值可以在路由範本中指定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-308">Default values can be specified in the route template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-309">`article` 路由參數透過在路由參數名稱之前加上雙星號 (`**`) 來定義為 *catch-all*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-309">The `article` route parameter is defined as a *catch-all* by the appearance of an double asterisk (`**`) before the route parameter name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-310">全部擷取路由參數會擷取 URL 路徑的其餘部分，而且也可以符合空字串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-310">Catch-all route parameters capture the remainder of the URL path and can also match the empty string.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-311">下列範例會新增路由條件約束和資料語彙基元：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-311">The following example adds route constraints and data tokens:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "us_english_products",
    template: "en-US/Products/{id}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Products", action = "Details" },
    constraints: new { id = new IntRouteConstraint() },
    dataTokens: new { locale = "en-US" });
```

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-312">上述範本會比對 `/en-US/Products/5` 等 URL 路徑，並擷取值 `{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 5 }` 和資料語彙基元 `{ locale = en-US }`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-312">The preceding template matches a URL path like `/en-US/Products/5` and extracts the values `{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 5 }` and the data tokens `{ locale = en-US }`.</span></span>

![[區域變數] 視窗語彙基元](routing/_static/tokens.png)

### <a name="route-class-url-generation"></a><span data-ttu-id="f01e9-314">路由類別 URL 產生</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-314">Route class URL generation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-315"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> 類別也可以結合一組路由值與其路由範本來產生 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-315">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> class can also perform URL generation by combining a set of route values with its route template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-316">這在邏輯上是比對 URL 路徑的反向處理序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-316">This is logically the reverse process of matching the URL path.</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-317">若要進一步了解 URL 產生，請假設您想要產生的 URL，並考慮路由範本將會如何比對該 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-317">To better understand URL generation, imagine what URL you want to generate and then think about how a route template would match that URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-318">產生的值為何？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-318">What values would be produced?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-319">這與 URL 產生在 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> 類別中的運作方式大致相同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-319">This is the rough equivalent of how URL generation works in the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> class.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-320">下列範例使用一般 ASP.NET Core MVC 預設路由：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-320">The following example uses a general ASP.NET Core MVC default route:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-321">路由值為 `{ controller = Products, action = List }` 時，會產生 URL `/Products/List`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-321">With the route values `{ controller = Products, action = List }`, the URL `/Products/List` is generated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-322">路由值會取代對應的路由參數，以形成 URL 路徑。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-322">The route values are substituted for the corresponding route parameters to form the URL path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-323">由於 `id` 是選擇性路由參數，因此沒有 `id` 值也可以成功產生 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-323">Since `id` is an optional route parameter, the URL is successfully generated without a value for `id`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-324">路由值為 `{ controller = Home, action = Index }` 時，會產生 URL `/`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-324">With the route values `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`, the URL `/` is generated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-325">所提供的路由值符合預設值，因此可以放心地省略這些預設值對應的區段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-325">The provided route values match the default values, and the segments corresponding to the default values are safely omitted.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-326">這兩個產生的 URL 會使用下列路由定義 (`/Home/Index` 和 `/`) 反覆存取，並產生用來產生 URL 的相同路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-326">Both URLs generated round-trip with the following route definition (`/Home/Index` and `/`) produce the same route values that were used to generate the URL.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-327">使用 ASP.NET Core MVC 的應用程式應該使用 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.Routing.UrlHelper> 來產生 URL，而不是直接呼叫路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-327">An app using ASP.NET Core MVC should use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.Routing.UrlHelper> to generate URLs instead of calling into routing directly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-328">如需 URL 產生的詳細資訊，請參閱 [URI 產生參考](#url-generation-reference)一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-328">For more information on URL generation, see the [Url generation reference](#url-generation-reference) section.</span></span>

## <a name="use-routing-middleware"></a><span data-ttu-id="f01e9-329">使用路由中介軟體</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-329">Use Routing Middleware</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-330">參考應用程式專案檔中的 [Microsoft.AspNetCore.App 中繼套件](xref:fundamentals/metapackage-app)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-330">Reference the [Microsoft.AspNetCore.App metapackage](xref:fundamentals/metapackage-app) in the app's project file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-331">在 `Startup.ConfigureServices` 中，將路由新增至服務容器：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-331">Add routing to the service container in `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/3.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_ConfigureServices&highlight=3)]

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-332">路由必須設定在 `Startup.Configure` 方法中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-332">Routes must be configured in the `Startup.Configure` method.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-333">範例應用程式使用下列 API：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-333">The sample app uses the following APIs:</span></span>

* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder>
* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-334"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> &ndash; 僅符合 HTTP GET 要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-334"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> &ndash; Matches only HTTP GET requests.</span></span>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RoutingBuilderExtensions.UseRouter*>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/3.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_RouteHandler)]

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-335">下表顯示使用指定 URL 的回應。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-335">The following table shows the responses with the given URIs.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-336">URI</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-336">URI</span></span>                    | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-337">回應</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-337">Response</span></span>                                          |
| ---------------------- | ------------------------------------------------- |
| `/package/create/3`    | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-338">Hello!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-338">Hello!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-339">Route values: [operation, create], [id, 3]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-339">Route values: [operation, create], [id, 3]</span></span> |
| `/package/track/-3`    | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-340">Hello!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-340">Hello!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-341">Route values: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-341">Route values: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span></span> |
| `/package/track/-3/`   | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-342">Hello!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-342">Hello!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-343">Route values: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-343">Route values: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span></span> |
| `/package/track/`      | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-344">要求失敗，沒有相符項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-344">The request falls through, no match.</span></span>              |
| `GET /hello/Joe`       | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-345">Hi, Joe!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-345">Hi, Joe!</span></span>                                          |
| `POST /hello/Joe`      | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-346">要求失敗，僅符合 HTTP GET。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-346">The request falls through, matches HTTP GET only.</span></span> |
| `GET /hello/Joe/Smith` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-347">要求失敗，沒有相符項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-347">The request falls through, no match.</span></span>              |

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-348">架構會提供一組擴充方法來建立路由 (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions>)：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-348">The framework provides a set of extension methods for creating routes (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions>):</span></span>

* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapDelete*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareDelete*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareGet*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewarePost*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewarePut*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareRoute*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareVerb*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPost*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPut*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapVerb*>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-349">`Map[Verb]` 方法會使用條件約束，將路由限制為方法名稱中的 HTTP 指令動詞。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-349">The `Map[Verb]` methods use constraints to limit the route to the HTTP Verb in the method name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-350">如需範例，請參閱 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> 與 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapVerb*>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-350">For example, see <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> and <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapVerb*>.</span></span>

## <a name="route-template-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="f01e9-351">路由範本參考</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-351">Route template reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-352">大括弧 (`{ ... }`) 內的語彙基元定義路由相符時會繫結的「路由參數」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-352">Tokens within curly braces (`{ ... }`) define *route parameters* that are bound if the route is matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-353">您可以在路由區段中定義多個路由參數，但其必須以常值分隔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-353">You can define more than one route parameter in a route segment, but they must be separated by a literal value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-354">例如，`{controller=Home}{action=Index}` 不是有效的路由，因為 `{controller}` 與 `{action}` 之間沒有任何常值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-354">For example, `{controller=Home}{action=Index}` isn't a valid route, since there's no literal value between `{controller}` and `{action}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-355">這些路由參數必須有一個名稱，並且可以指定其他屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-355">These route parameters must have a name and may have additional attributes specified.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-356">路由參數之外的常值文字 (例如，`{id}`) 和路徑分隔符號 `/` 必須符合 URL 中的文字。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-356">Literal text other than route parameters (for example, `{id}`) and the path separator `/` must match the text in the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-357">文字比對會區分大小寫，並以 URL 路徑的已解碼表示法為基礎。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-357">Text matching is case-insensitive and based on the decoded representation of the URLs path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-358">若要比對常值路由參數分隔符號 (`{` 或 `}`)，請重複字元 (`{{` 或 `}}`) 來將分隔符號逸出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-358">To match a literal route parameter delimiter (`{` or `}`), escape the delimiter by repeating the character (`{{` or `}}`).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-359">URL 模式嘗試擷取具有選擇性副檔名的檔案名稱時，具有其他考量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-359">URL patterns that attempt to capture a file name with an optional file extension have additional considerations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-360">以範本 `files/{filename}.{ext?}` 為例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-360">For example, consider the template `files/{filename}.{ext?}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-361">當 `filename` 和 `ext` 都存在值時，就會填入這兩個值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-361">When values for both `filename` and `ext` exist, both values are populated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-362">如果 URL 中只有 `filename` 存在值，由於結尾的句點 (`.`) 是選擇性項目，因此路由相符。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-362">If only a value for `filename` exists in the URL, the route matches because the trailing period (`.`) is  optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-363">下列 URL 符合此路由：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-363">The following URLs match this route:</span></span>

* `/files/myFile.txt`
* `/files/myFile`

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-364">您可以使用一個星號 (`*`) 或雙星號 (`**`) 作為路由參數的前置詞，以繫結至 URI 的其餘部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-364">You can use an asterisk (`*`) or double asterisk (`**`) as a prefix to a route parameter to bind to the rest of the URI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-365">這稱為 *catch-all* 參數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-365">These are called a *catch-all* parameters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-366">例如，`blog/{**slug}` 符合以 `/blog` 開頭且其後有任何值 (這會指派給 `slug` 路由值) 的所有 URI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-366">For example, `blog/{**slug}` matches any URI that starts with `/blog` and has any value following it, which is assigned to the `slug` route value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-367">全部擷取參數也可以符合空字串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-367">Catch-all parameters can also match the empty string.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-368">當使用路由產生 URL (包括路徑分隔符號 (`/`) 字元) 時，catch-all 參數會逸出適當的字元。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-368">The catch-all parameter escapes the appropriate characters when the route is used to generate a URL, including path separator (`/`) characters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-369">例如，路由值為 `{ path = "my/path" }` 的路由 `foo/{*path}` 會產生 `foo/my%2Fpath`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-369">For example, the route `foo/{*path}` with route values `{ path = "my/path" }` generates `foo/my%2Fpath`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-370">請注意逸出的斜線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-370">Note the escaped forward slash.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-371">若要反覆存取路徑分隔符號字元，請使用 `**` 路由參數前置詞。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-371">To round-trip path separator characters, use the `**` route parameter prefix.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-372">具有 `{ path = "my/path" }` 的路由 `foo/{**path}` 會產生 `foo/my/path`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-372">The route `foo/{**path}` with `{ path = "my/path" }` generates `foo/my/path`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-373">路由參數可能有「預設值」，指定方法是在參數名稱之後指定預設值，並以等號 (`=`) 分隔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-373">Route parameters may have *default values* designated by specifying the default value after the parameter name separated by an equals sign (`=`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-374">例如，`{controller=Home}` 定義 `Home` 作為 `controller` 的預設值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-374">For example, `{controller=Home}` defines `Home` as the default value for `controller`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-375">如果 URL 中沒有用於參數的任何值，則會使用預設值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-375">The default value is used if no value is present in the URL for the parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-376">路由參數也可以設為選擇性，方法是在參數名稱結尾附加問號 (`?`)，如 `id?` 中所示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-376">Route parameters are made optional by appending a question mark (`?`) to the end of the parameter name, as in `id?`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-377">選擇性值與預設路由參數之間的差異在於，具有預設值的路由參數一定會產生值&mdash;選擇性參數只有在要求 URL 提供值時才會有值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-377">The difference between optional values and default route parameters is that a route parameter with a default value always produces a value&mdash;an optional parameter has a value only when a value is provided by the request URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-378">路由參數可能具有條件約束，這些條件約束必須符合與 URL 繫結的路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-378">Route parameters may have constraints that must match the route value bound from the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-379">在路由參數名稱之後新增分號 (`:`) 和條件約束名稱，即可指定路由參數的「內嵌條件約束」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-379">Adding a colon (`:`) and constraint name after the route parameter name specifies an *inline constraint* on a route parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-380">如果條件約束需要引數，這些引數會在條件約束名稱後面以括弧 (`(...)`) 括住。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-380">If the constraint requires arguments, they're enclosed in parentheses (`(...)`) after the constraint name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-381">指定多個內嵌條件約束的方法是附加另一個冒號 (`:`) 和條件約束名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-381">Multiple inline constraints can be specified by appending another colon (`:`) and constraint name.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-382">條件約束名稱和引述會傳遞至 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IInlineConstraintResolver> 服務來建立 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> 的執行個體，以用於 URL 處理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-382">The constraint name and arguments are passed to the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IInlineConstraintResolver> service to create an instance of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> to use in URL processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-383">例如，路由範本 `blog/{article:minlength(10)}` 指定具有引數 `10` 的 `minlength` 條件約束。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-383">For example, the route template `blog/{article:minlength(10)}` specifies a `minlength` constraint with the argument `10`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-384">如需路由條件約束詳細資訊和架構所提供的條件約束清單，請參閱[路由條件約束參考](#route-constraint-reference)一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-384">For more information on route constraints and a list of the constraints provided by the framework, see the [Route constraint reference](#route-constraint-reference) section.</span></span>
