<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-385">路由參數也可以具有參數轉換器，以在產生連結及根據 URL 比對動作和頁面時，轉換參數的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-385">Route parameters may also have parameter transformers, which transform a parameter's value when generating links and matching actions and pages to URLs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-386">與條件約束類似，可以透過在路徑參數名稱後面新增冒號 (`:`) 和轉換器名稱，將參數轉換器內嵌新增至路徑參數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-386">Like constraints, parameter transformers can be added inline to a route parameter by adding a colon (`:`) and transformer name after the route parameter name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-387">例如，路由範本 `blog/{article:slugify}` 會指定 `slugify` 轉換器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-387">For example, the route template `blog/{article:slugify}` specifies a `slugify` transformer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-388">如需參數轉換器的詳細資訊，請參閱[參數轉器參考](#parameter-transformer-reference)一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-388">For more information on parameter transformers, see the [Parameter transformer reference](#parameter-transformer-reference) section.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-389">下表示範範例路由範本及其行為。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-389">The following table demonstrates example route templates and their behavior.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-390">路由範本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-390">Route Template</span></span>                           | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-391">範例比對 URI</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-391">Example Matching URI</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-392">要求 URI&hellip;</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-392">The request URI&hellip;</span></span>                                                    |
| ---------------------------------------- | ----------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `hello`                                  | `/hello`                | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-393">只比對單一路徑 `/hello`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-393">Only matches the single path `/hello`.</span></span>                                     |
| `{Page=Home}`                            | `/`                     | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-394">比對並將 `Page` 設定為 `Home`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-394">Matches and sets `Page` to `Home`.</span></span>                                         |
| `{Page=Home}`                            | `/Contact`              | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-395">比對並將 `Page` 設定為 `Contact`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-395">Matches and sets `Page` to `Contact`.</span></span>                                      |
| `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`            | `/Products/List`        | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-396">對應至 `Products` 控制器和 `List` 動作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-396">Maps to the `Products` controller and `List` action.</span></span>                       |
| `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`            | `/Products/Details/123` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-397">對應至 `Products` 控制器和 `Details` 動作 (`id` 設定為 123)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-397">Maps to the `Products` controller and  `Details` action (`id` set to 123).</span></span> |
| `{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}` | `/`                     | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-398">對應至 `Home` 控制器和 `Index` 方法 (會忽略 `id`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-398">Maps to the `Home` controller and `Index` method (`id` is ignored).</span></span>        |

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-399">使用範本通常是最簡單的路由方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-399">Using a template is generally the simplest approach to routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-400">條件約束和預設值也可以在路由範本外部指定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-400">Constraints and defaults can also be specified outside the route template.</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-401">啟用[記錄](xref:fundamentals/logging/index)以查看內建路由實作 (例如 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>) 如何符合要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-401">Enable [Logging](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) to see how the built-in routing implementations, such as <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>, match requests.</span></span>

## <a name="reserved-routing-names"></a><span data-ttu-id="f01e9-402">保留的路由名稱</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-402">Reserved routing names</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-403">下列關鍵字是保留的名稱，不能用作路由名稱或參數：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-403">The following keywords are reserved names and can't be used as route names or parameters:</span></span>

* `action`
* `area`
* `controller`
* `handler`
* `page`

## <a name="route-constraint-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="f01e9-404">路由條件約束參考</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-404">Route constraint reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-405">路由條件約束執行時機是出現符合傳入 URL 的項目，並將 URL 路徑語彙基元化成路由值時。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-405">Route constraints execute when a match has occurred to the incoming URL and the URL path is tokenized into route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-406">路由條件約束通常會透過路由範本檢查相關聯的路由值，並對是否可接受值做出是/否決策。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-406">Route constraints generally inspect the route value associated via the route template and make a yes/no decision about whether or not the value is acceptable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-407">某些路由條件約束會使用路由值以外的資料，以考慮是否可以路由要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-407">Some route constraints use data outside the route value to consider whether the request can be routed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-408">例如，<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Constraints.HttpMethodRouteConstraint> 可以依據其 HTTP 指令動詞接受或拒絕要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-408">For example, the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Constraints.HttpMethodRouteConstraint> can accept or reject a request based on its HTTP verb.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-409">條件約束可用於路由要求和連結產生。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-409">Constraints are used in routing requests and link generation.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-410">請勿針對**輸入驗證**使用條件約束。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-410">Don't use constraints for **input validation**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-411">如果針對**輸入驗證**使用條件約束，則無效的輸入會導致產生「404 - 找不到」回應，而不是「400 - 錯誤要求」與適當的錯誤訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-411">If constraints are used for **input validation**, invalid input results in a *404 - Not Found* response instead of a *400 - Bad Request* with an appropriate error message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-412">路由條件約束會用來**釐清**類似的路由，而不是用來驗證特定路由的輸入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-412">Route constraints are used to **disambiguate** similar routes, not to validate the inputs for a particular route.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-413">下表示範範例路由條件約束及其預期行為。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-413">The following table demonstrates example route constraints and their expected behavior.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-414">條件約束</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-414">constraint</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-415">範例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-415">Example</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-416">範例相符項目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-416">Example Matches</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-417">注意事項</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-417">Notes</span></span> |
| ---------- | ------- | --------------- | ----- |
| `int` | `{id:int}` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-418">`123456789`、 `-123456789`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-418">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-419">符合任何整數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-419">Matches any integer</span></span> |
| `bool` | `{active:bool}` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-420">`true`、 `FALSE`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-420">`true`, `FALSE`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-421">符合 `true` 或 `false` (不區分大小寫)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-421">Matches `true` or `false` (case-insensitive)</span></span> |
| `datetime` | `{dob:datetime}` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-422">`2016-12-31`、 `2016-12-31 7:32pm`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-422">`2016-12-31`, `2016-12-31 7:32pm`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-423">符合有效的 `DateTime` 值 (在不因國別而異的文化特性中 - 請參閱警告)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-423">Matches a valid `DateTime` value (in the invariant culture - see warning)</span></span> |
| `decimal` | `{price:decimal}` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-424">`49.99`、 `-1,000.01`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-424">`49.99`, `-1,000.01`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-425">符合有效的 `decimal` 值 (在不因國別而異的文化特性中 - 請參閱警告)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-425">Matches a valid `decimal` value (in the invariant culture - see warning)</span></span> |
| `double` | `{weight:double}` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-426">`1.234`、 `-1,001.01e8`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-426">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-427">符合有效的 `double` 值 (在不因國別而異的文化特性中 - 請參閱警告)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-427">Matches a valid `double` value (in the invariant culture - see warning)</span></span> |
| `float` | `{weight:float}` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-428">`1.234`、 `-1,001.01e8`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-428">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-429">符合有效的 `float` 值 (在不因國別而異的文化特性中 - 請參閱警告)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-429">Matches a valid `float` value (in the invariant culture - see warning)</span></span> |
| `guid` | `{id:guid}` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-430">`CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638`、 `{CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638}`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-430">`CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638`, `{CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638}`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-431">符合有效的 `Guid` 值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-431">Matches a valid `Guid` value</span></span> |
| `long` | `{ticks:long}` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-432">`123456789`、 `-123456789`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-432">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-433">符合有效的 `long` 值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-433">Matches a valid `long` value</span></span> |
| `minlength(value)` | `{username:minlength(4)}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-434">字串必須至少有 4 個字元</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-434">String must be at least 4 characters</span></span> |
| `maxlength(value)` | `{filename:maxlength(8)}` | `Richard` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-435">字串不能超過 8 個字元</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-435">String must be no more than 8 characters</span></span> |
| `length(length)` | `{filename:length(12)}` | `somefile.txt` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-436">字串長度必須剛好是 12 個字元</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-436">String must be exactly 12 characters long</span></span> |
| `length(min,max)` | `{filename:length(8,16)}` | `somefile.txt` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-437">字串長度必須至少有 8 個字元，但不能超過 16 個字元</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-437">String must be at least 8 and no more than 16 characters long</span></span> |
| `min(value)` | `{age:min(18)}` | `19` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-438">整數值必須至少為 18</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-438">Integer value must be at least 18</span></span> |
| `max(value)` | `{age:max(120)}` | `91` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-439">整數值不能超過 120</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-439">Integer value must be no more than 120</span></span> |
| `range(min,max)` | `{age:range(18,120)}` | `91` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-440">整數值必須至少為 18，但不能超過 120</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-440">Integer value must be at least 18 but no more than 120</span></span> |
| `alpha` | `{name:alpha}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-441">字串必須包含一或多個字母字元 (`a`-`z`，不區分大小寫)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-441">String must consist of one or more alphabetical characters (`a`-`z`, case-insensitive)</span></span> |
| `regex(expression)` | `{ssn:regex(^\\d{{3}}-\\d{{2}}-\\d{{4}}$)}` | `123-45-6789` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-442">字串必須符合規則運算式 (請參閱有關定義規則運算式的提示)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-442">String must match the regular expression (see tips about defining a regular expression)</span></span> |
| `required` | `{name:required}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-443">用來強制執行在 URL 產生期間呈現非參數值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-443">Used to enforce that a non-parameter value is present during URL generation</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-444">以冒號分隔的多個條件約束，可以套用至單一參數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-444">Multiple, colon-delimited constraints can be applied to a single parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-445">例如，下列條件約束會將參數限制在 1 或更大的整數值：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-445">For example, the following constraint restricts a parameter to an integer value of 1 or greater:</span></span>

```csharp
[Route("users/{id:int:min(1)}")]
public User GetUserById(int id) { }
```

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-446">確認 URL 可以轉換成 CLR 類型的路由條件約束 (例如 `int` 或 `DateTime`) 一律使用不因國別而異的文化特性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-446">Route constraints that verify the URL and are converted to a CLR type (such as `int` or `DateTime`) always use the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-447">這些條件約束假設 URL 不可當地語系化。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-447">These constraints assume that the URL is non-localizable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-448">架構提供的路由條件約束不會修改路由值中儲存的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-448">The framework-provided route constraints don't modify the values stored in route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-449">所有從 URL 剖析而來的路由值會儲存為字串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-449">All route values parsed from the URL are stored as strings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-450">例如，`float` 條件約束會嘗試將路由值轉換成浮點數，但轉換的值只能用來確認它可以轉換成浮點數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-450">For example, the `float` constraint attempts to convert the route value to a float, but the converted value is used only to verify it can be converted to a float.</span></span>

## <a name="regular-expressions"></a><span data-ttu-id="f01e9-451">規則運算式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-451">Regular expressions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-452">ASP.NET Core 架構將 `RegexOptions.IgnoreCase | RegexOptions.Compiled | RegexOptions.CultureInvariant` 新增至規則運算式建構函式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-452">The ASP.NET Core framework adds `RegexOptions.IgnoreCase | RegexOptions.Compiled | RegexOptions.CultureInvariant` to the regular expression constructor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-453">如需這些成員的說明，請參閱 <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.RegexOptions>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-453">See <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.RegexOptions> for a description of these members.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-454">規則運算式使用的分隔符號和語彙基元，類似於路由和 C# 語言所使用的分隔符號和語彙基元。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-454">Regular expressions use delimiters and tokens similar to those used by Routing and the C# language.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-455">規則運算式的語彙基元必須逸出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-455">Regular expression tokens must be escaped.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-456">若要在路由中使用規則運算式 `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$`，運算式必須以字串中所提供的 `\` (單一反斜線) 字元作為 C# 原始程式檔中的 `\\` (雙反斜線) 字元，才能逸出 `\` 字串逸出字元 (除非使用[逐字字串常值](/dotnet/csharp/language-reference/keywords/string))。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-456">To use the regular expression `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` in routing, the expression must have the `\` (single backslash) characters provided in the string as `\\` (double backslash) characters in the C# source file in order to escape the `\` string escape character (unless using [verbatim string literals](/dotnet/csharp/language-reference/keywords/string)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-457">若要逸出路由參數分隔符號字元 (`{`、`}`、`[`、`]`)，請在運算式中使用雙字元 (`{{`、`}`、`[[`、`]]`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-457">To escape routing parameter delimiter characters (`{`, `}`, `[`, `]`), double the characters in the expression (`{{`, `}`, `[[`, `]]`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-458">下表顯示規則運算式和逸出的版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-458">The following table shows a regular expression and the escaped version.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-459">規則運算式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-459">Regular Expression</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-460">逸出的規則運算式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-460">Escaped Regular Expression</span></span>     |
| --------------------- | ------------------------------ |
| `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` | `^\\d{{3}}-\\d{{2}}-\\d{{4}}$` |
| `^[a-z]{2}$`          | `^[[a-z]]{{2}}$`               |

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-461">路由中所使用的規則運算式通常以插入號 (`^`) 字元開頭，並符合字串的開始位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-461">Regular expressions used in routing often start with the caret (`^`) character and match starting position of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-462">運算式通常以貨幣符號 (`$`) 字元結尾，並符合字串的結尾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-462">The expressions often end with the dollar sign (`$`) character and match end of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-463">`^` 和 `$` 字元可確保規則運算式符合整個路由參數值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-463">The `^` and `$` characters ensure that the regular expression match the entire route parameter value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-464">若不使用 `^` 與 `$` 字元，規則運算式會比對字串內的所有部分字串，這通常不是您想要的結果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-464">Without the `^` and `$` characters, the regular expression match any substring within the string, which is often undesirable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-465">下表提供範例，並說明它們符合或無法符合的原因。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-465">The following table provides examples and explains why they match or fail to match.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-466">運算式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-466">Expression</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-467">字串</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-467">String</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-468">比對</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-468">Match</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-469">註解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-469">Comment</span></span>               |
| ------------ | --------- | :---: |  -------------------- |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-470">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-470">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-471">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-471">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-472">子字串相符項目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-472">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-473">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-473">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-474">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-474">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-475">子字串相符項目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-475">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-476">mz</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-476">mz</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-477">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-477">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-478">符合運算式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-478">Matches expression</span></span>    |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-479">MZ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-479">MZ</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-480">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-480">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-481">不區分大小寫</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-481">Not case sensitive</span></span>    |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-482">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-482">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-483">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-483">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-484">請參閱上述的 `^` 和 `$`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-484">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-485">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-485">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-486">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-486">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-487">請參閱上述的 `^` 和 `$`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-487">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-488">如需規則運算式語法的詳細資訊，請參閱 [.NET Framework 規則運算式](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-488">For more information on regular expression syntax, see [.NET Framework Regular Expressions](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-489">若要將參數限制為一組已知的可能值，請使用規則運算式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-489">To constrain a parameter to a known set of possible values, use a regular expression.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-490">例如，`{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}` 只會將 `action` 路由值與 `list`、`get` 或 `create` 相符。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-490">For example, `{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}` only matches the `action` route value to `list`, `get`, or `create`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-491">如果已傳入條件約束字典，字串 `^(list|get|create)$` 則是對等項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-491">If passed into the constraints dictionary, the string `^(list|get|create)$` is equivalent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-492">已傳入條件約束字典 (未內嵌在範本內) 的條件約束，即使不符合其中一個已知的條件約束，也會被視為規則運算式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-492">Constraints that are passed in the constraints dictionary (not inline within a template) that don't match one of the known constraints are also treated as regular expressions.</span></span>

## <a name="custom-route-constraints"></a><span data-ttu-id="f01e9-493">自訂路由限制式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-493">Custom Route Constraints</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-494">除了內建的路由限制式之外，自訂路由限制式也可以透過實作 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> 介面來建立。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-494">In addition to the built-in route constraints, custom route constraints can be created by implementing the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> interface.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-495"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> 介面包含單一方法 `Match`，此方法會在滿足限制式時傳回 `true`，否則會傳回 `false`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-495">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> interface contains a single method, `Match`, which returns `true` if the constraint is satisfied and `false` otherwise.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-496">若要使用自訂 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>，路由限制式型別必須必須向應用程式的 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> (在應用程式的服務容器中) 註冊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-496">To use a custom <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>, the route constraint type must be registered with the app's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> in the app's service container.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-497"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> 是一個目錄，它將路由限制式機碼對應到可驗證那些限制式的 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> 實作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-497">A <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> is a dictionary that maps route constraint keys to <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> implementations that validate those constraints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-498">更新應用程式的 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> 時，可在 `Startup.ConfigureServices` 中於進行 [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) 呼叫時更新，或透過使用 `services.Configure<RouteOptions>` 直接設定 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions> 來更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-498">An app's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> can be updated in `Startup.ConfigureServices` either as part of a [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) call or by configuring <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions> directly with `services.Configure<RouteOptions>`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-499">例如：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-499">For example:</span></span>

```csharp
services.AddRouting(options =>
{
    options.ConstraintMap.Add("customName", typeof(MyCustomConstraint));
});
```

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-500">限制式接著能以一般方式套用到路由 (使用註冊限制式型別時使用名稱)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-500">The constraint can then be applied to routes in the usual manner, using the name specified when registering the constraint type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-501">例如：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-501">For example:</span></span>

```csharp
[HttpGet("{id:customName}")]
public ActionResult<string> Get(string id)
```

## <a name="parameter-transformer-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="f01e9-502">參數轉換器參考</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-502">Parameter transformer reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-503">參數轉換程式：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-503">Parameter transformers:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-504">會在為 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> 產生連結時執行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-504">Execute when generating a link for a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-505">實作 `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IOutboundParameterTransformer`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-505">Implement `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IOutboundParameterTransformer`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-506">是使用 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> 進行設定的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-506">Are configured using <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-507">採用參數的路由值，並將它轉換為新的字串值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-507">Take the parameter's route value and transform it to a new string value.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-508">導致在所產生連結中使用已轉換的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-508">Result in using the transformed value in the generated link.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-509">例如，具有 `Url.Action(new { article = "MyTestArticle" })` 之路由模式 `blog\{article:slugify}` 中的自訂 `slugify` 參數轉換器，會產生 `blog\my-test-article`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-509">For example, a custom `slugify` parameter transformer in route pattern `blog\{article:slugify}` with `Url.Action(new { article = "MyTestArticle" })` generates `blog\my-test-article`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-510">若要在路由模式中使用參數轉換器，請先在 `Startup.ConfigureServices` 中使用 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> 進行設定：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-510">To use a parameter transformer in a route pattern, configure it first using <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> in `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span></span>

```csharp
services.AddRouting(options =>
{
    // Replace the type and the name used to refer to it with your own
    // IOutboundParameterTransformer implementation
    options.ConstraintMap["slugify"] = typeof(SlugifyParameterTransformer);
});
```

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-511">架構會使用參數轉換器來轉換端點解析的 URI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-511">Parameter transformers are used by the framework to transform the URI where an endpoint resolves.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-512">例如，ASP.NET Core MVC 會使用參數轉換器，轉換用於比對 `area`、`controller`、`action` 和 `page` 的路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-512">For example, ASP.NET Core MVC uses parameter transformers to transform the route value used to match an `area`, `controller`, `action`, and `page`.</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller:slugify=Home}/{action:slugify=Index}/{id?}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-513">使用上述的路由，動作 `SubscriptionManagementController.GetAll()` 會與URI `/subscription-management/get-all` 比對。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-513">With the preceding route, the action `SubscriptionManagementController.GetAll()` is matched with the URI `/subscription-management/get-all`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-514">參數轉換器不會變更用來產生連結的路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-514">A parameter transformer doesn't change the route values used to generate a link.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-515">例如，`Url.Action("GetAll", "SubscriptionManagement")` 會輸出 `/subscription-management/get-all`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-515">For example, `Url.Action("GetAll", "SubscriptionManagement")` outputs `/subscription-management/get-all`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-516">ASP.NET Core 針對搭配產生的路由使用參數轉換程式提供了 API 慣例：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-516">ASP.NET Core provides API conventions for using a parameter transformers with generated routes:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-517">ASP.NET Core MVC 有 `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.RouteTokenTransformerConvention` API 慣例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-517">ASP.NET Core MVC has the `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.RouteTokenTransformerConvention` API convention.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-518">此慣例會將所指定參數轉換程式套用到應用程式中的所有屬性路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-518">This convention applies a specified parameter transformer to all attribute routes in the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-519">參數轉換程式會在被取代時轉換屬性路由語彙基元。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-519">The parameter transformer transforms attribute route tokens as they are replaced.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-520">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[使用參數轉換程式自訂語彙基元取代](/aspnet/core/mvc/controllers/routing#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-token-replacement)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-520">For more information, see [Use a parameter transformer to customize token replacement](/aspnet/core/mvc/controllers/routing#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-token-replacement).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-521">Razor Pages 有 `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.PageRouteTransformerConvention` API 慣例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-521">Razor Pages has the `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.PageRouteTransformerConvention` API convention.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-522">此慣例會將所指定參數轉換器套用至所有自動探索到的 Razor Pages。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-522">This convention applies a specified parameter transformer to all automatically discovered Razor Pages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-523">參數轉換器會轉換 Razor Pages 路由的資料夾與檔案名稱區段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-523">The parameter transformer transforms the folder and file name segments of Razor Pages routes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-524">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[使用參數轉換程式自訂頁面路由](/aspnet/core/razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-page-routes)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-524">For more information, see [Use a parameter transformer to customize page routes](/aspnet/core/razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-page-routes).</span></span>

## <a name="url-generation-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="f01e9-525">URL 產生參考</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-525">URL generation reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-526">下列範例示範如何在指定路由值字典和 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteCollection> 的情況下產生路由的連結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-526">The following example shows how to generate a link to a route given a dictionary of route values and a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteCollection>.</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/3.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_Dictionary)]

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-527">在上述範例的結尾產生的 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath> 是 `/package/create/123`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-527">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath> generated at the end of the preceding sample is `/package/create/123`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-528">字典提供「追蹤套件路由」範本 `package/{operation}/{id}` 的 `operation` 和 `id` 路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-528">The dictionary supplies the `operation` and `id` route values of the "Track Package Route" template, `package/{operation}/{id}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-529">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[使用路由中介軟體](#use-routing-middleware)一節或[範例應用程式](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples)中的範例程式碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-529">For details, see the sample code in the [Use Routing Middleware](#use-routing-middleware) section or the [sample app](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-530"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext> 建構函式的第二個參數是「環境值」的集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-530">The second parameter to the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext> constructor is a collection of *ambient values*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-531">環境值便於使用，因為它們會限制開發人員必須在要求內容中指定的值數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-531">Ambient values are convenient to use because they limit the number of values a developer must specify within a request context.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-532">目前要求的目前路由值被視為用於連結產生的環境值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-532">The current route values of the current request are considered ambient values for link generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-533">在 ASP.NET Core MVC 應用程式 `HomeController` 的 `About` 動作中，您不需要指定控制器路由值以連結到 `Index` 動作&mdash;會使用 `Home` 的環境值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-533">In an ASP.NET Core MVC app's `About` action of the `HomeController`, you don't need to specify the controller route value to link to the `Index` action&mdash;the ambient value of `Home` is used.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-534">不符合參數的環境值會予以忽略。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-534">Ambient values that don't match a parameter are ignored.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-535">當明確提供的值覆寫環境值時，也會忽略環境值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-535">Ambient values are also ignored when an explicitly provided value overrides the ambient value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-536">URL 中的比對是從左到右。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-536">Matching occurs from left to right in the URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-537">明確提供但不符合路由區段的值會新增至查詢字串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-537">Values explicitly provided but that don't match a segment of the route are added to the query string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-538">下表顯示使用路由範本 `{controller}/{action}/{id?}` 時的結果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-538">The following table shows the result when using the route template `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-539">環境值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-539">Ambient Values</span></span>                     | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-540">明確值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-540">Explicit Values</span></span>                        | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-541">結果</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-541">Result</span></span>                  |
| ---------------------------------- | -------------------------------------- | ----------------------- |
| <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-542">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-542">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-543">action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-543">action = "About"</span></span>                       | `/Home/About`           |
| <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-544">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-544">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-545">controller = "Order", action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-545">controller = "Order", action = "About"</span></span> | `/Order/About`          |
| <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-546">controller = "Home", color = "Red"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-546">controller = "Home", color = "Red"</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-547">action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-547">action = "About"</span></span>                       | `/Home/About`           |
| <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-548">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-548">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-549">action = "About", color = "Red"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-549">action = "About", color = "Red"</span></span>        | `/Home/About?color=Red` |

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-550">如果路由具有未對應至參數的預設值，且該值會明確提供，它必須符合預設值：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-550">If a route has a default value that doesn't correspond to a parameter and that value is explicitly provided, it must match the default value:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute("blog_route", "blog/{*slug}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Blog", action = "ReadPost" });
```

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-551">連結產生只有在提供了 `controller` 與 `action` 的相符值時，才會產生此路由的連結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-551">Link generation only generates a link for this route when the matching values for `controller` and `action` are provided.</span></span>

## <a name="complex-segments"></a><span data-ttu-id="f01e9-552">複雜區段</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-552">Complex segments</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-553">複雜區段 (例如，`[Route("/x{token}y")]`) 會透過以非窮盡的方式，由右至左比對常值來處理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-553">Complex segments (for example `[Route("/x{token}y")]`) are processed by matching up literals from right to left in a non-greedy way.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-554">請參閱[此程式碼](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293)以了解如何比對複雜區段的詳細解釋。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-554">See [this code](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) for a detailed explanation of how complex segments are matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-555">[程式法範例](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293)不是由 ASP.NET Core 使用，但它提供一個好的複雜區段解釋。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-555">The [code sample](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) is not used by ASP.NET Core, but it provides a good explanation of complex segments.</span></span>
<!-- While that code is no longer used by ASP.NET Core for complex segment matching, it provides a good match to the current algorithm. The [current code](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore/blob/91514c9af7e0f4c44029b51f05a01c6fe4c96e4c/src/Http/Routing/src/Matching/DfaMatcherBuilder.cs#L227-L244) is too abstracted from matching to be useful for understanding complex segment matching.

## <a name="configuring-endpoint-metadata"></a><span data-ttu-id="f01e9-556">設定端點中繼資料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-556">Configuring endpoint metadata</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-557">下列連結提供設定端點中繼資料的相關資訊：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-557">The following links provide information on configuring endpoint metadata:</span></span>

<a name="hostmatch"></a>

## <a name="host-matching-in-routes-with-requirehost"></a><span data-ttu-id="f01e9-563">搭配 RequireHost 的路由中的主機比對</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-563">Host matching in routes with RequireHost</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-564">`RequireHost` 將條件約束套用至需要指定之主機的路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-564">`RequireHost` applies a constraint to the route which requires the specified host.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-565">`RequireHost` 或 `[Host]` 參數可以是：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-565">The `RequireHost` or `[Host]` parameter can be:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-566">主機： `www.domain.com` （符合任何埠的 `www.domain.com`）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-566">Host: `www.domain.com` (matches `www.domain.com` with any port)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-567">具有萬用字元的主機： `*.domain.com` （符合任何埠上的 `www.domain.com`、`subdomain.domain.com`或 `www.subdomain.domain.com`）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-567">Host with wildcard: `*.domain.com` (matches `www.domain.com`, `subdomain.domain.com`, or `www.subdomain.domain.com` on any port)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-568">埠： `*:5000` （符合任何主機的通訊埠5000）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-568">Port: `*:5000` (matches port 5000 with any host)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-569">主機和埠： `www.domain.com:5000`、`*.domain.com:5000` （符合主機和埠）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-569">Host and port: `www.domain.com:5000`, `*.domain.com:5000` (matches host and port)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-570">您可以使用 `RequireHost` 或 `[Host]`來指定多個參數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-570">Multiple parameters can be specified using `RequireHost` or `[Host]`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-571">條件約束會符合任何參數的有效主機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-571">The constraint will match hosts valid for any of the parameters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-572">例如，`[Host("domain.com", "*.domain.com")]` 會符合 `domain.com`、`www.domain.com`或 `subdomain.domain.com`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-572">For example, `[Host("domain.com", "*.domain.com")]` will match `domain.com`, `www.domain.com`, or `subdomain.domain.com`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-573">下列程式碼會使用 `RequireHost` 來要求路由上指定的主機：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-573">The following code uses `RequireHost` to require the specified host on the route:</span></span>

```csharp
public void Configure(IApplicationBuilder app)
{
    app.UseRouting();

    app.UseEndpoints(endpoints =>
    {
        endpoints.MapGet("/", context => context.Response.WriteAsync("Hi Contoso!"))
            .RequireHost("contoso.com");
        endpoints.MapGet("/", context => context.Response.WriteAsync("Hi AdventureWorks!"))
            .RequireHost("adventure-works.com");
        endpoints.MapHealthChecks("/healthz").RequireHost("*:8080");
    });
}
```

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-574">下列程式碼會使用 `[Host]` 屬性來要求控制器上的指定主機：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-574">The following code uses the `[Host]` attribute to require the specified host on the controller:</span></span>

```csharp
[Host("contoso.com", "adventure-works.com")]
public class HomeController : Controller
{
    private readonly ILogger<HomeController> _logger;

    public HomeController(ILogger<HomeController> logger)
    {
        _logger = logger;
    }

    public IActionResult Index()
    {
        return View();
    }

    [Host("example.com:8080")]
    public IActionResult Privacy()
    {
        return View();
    }

}
```

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-575">當 `[Host]` 屬性同時套用至控制器和動作方法時：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-575">When the `[Host]` attribute is applied to both the controller and action method:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-576">會使用動作上的屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-576">The attribute on the action is used.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-577">已忽略控制器屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-577">The controller attribute is ignored.</span></span>

::: moniker-end

::: moniker range="= aspnetcore-2.2"

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-578">路由會負責將要求 Uri 對應至端點，並將傳入要求分派至這些端點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-578">Routing is responsible for mapping request URIs to endpoints and dispatching incoming requests to those endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-579">路由定義於應用程式，並在該應用程式啟動時進行設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-579">Routes are defined in the app and configured when the app starts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-580">路由可以選擇性地從要求中所包含的 URL 擷取值，然後這些值就可用於處理要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-580">A route can optionally extract values from the URL contained in the request, and these values can then be used for request processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-581">使用來自應用程式的路由資訊，路由也能夠產生對應至端點的 Url。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-581">Using route information from the app, routing is also able to generate URLs that map to endpoints.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-582">若要使用 ASP.NET Core 2.2 中的最新路由情節，請將[相容性版本](xref:mvc/compatibility-version)指定為 `Startup.ConfigureServices` 中的 MVC 服務註冊：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-582">To use the latest routing scenarios in ASP.NET Core 2.2, specify the [compatibility version](xref:mvc/compatibility-version) to the MVC services registration in `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span></span>

```csharp
services.AddMvc()
    .SetCompatibilityVersion(CompatibilityVersion.Version_2_2);
```

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-583"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.MvcOptions.EnableEndpointRouting> 選項會決定路由功能應該在內部使用以端點為基礎的邏輯，或以 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter> 為基礎的邏輯 (適用於 ASP.NET Core 2.1 或更舊版本)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-583">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.MvcOptions.EnableEndpointRouting> option determines if routing should internally use endpoint-based logic or the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>-based logic of ASP.NET Core 2.1 or earlier.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-584">當相容性版本設定為 2.2 或更新版本時，預設值為 `true`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-584">When the compatibility version is set to 2.2 or later, the default value is `true`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-585">將值設定為 `false` 可使用舊版路由邏輯：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-585">Set the value to `false` to use the prior routing logic:</span></span>

```csharp
// Use the routing logic of ASP.NET Core 2.1 or earlier:
services.AddMvc(options => options.EnableEndpointRouting = false)
    .SetCompatibilityVersion(CompatibilityVersion.Version_2_2);
```

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-586">如需以 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter> 為基礎之路由的詳細資訊，請參閱[本主題的 ASP.NET Core 2.1 版本](/aspnet/core/fundamentals/routing?view=aspnetcore-2.1)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-586">For more information on <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>-based routing, see the [ASP.NET Core 2.1 version of this topic](/aspnet/core/fundamentals/routing?view=aspnetcore-2.1).</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-587">本文件涵蓋低階的 ASP.NET Core 路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-587">This document covers low-level ASP.NET Core routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-588">如需 ASP.NET Core MVC 路由的資訊，請參閱 <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-588">For information on ASP.NET Core MVC routing, see <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-589">如需 Razor Pages 中路由慣例的資訊，請參閱 <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-589">For information on routing conventions in Razor Pages, see <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-590">[檢視或下載範例程式碼](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples) \(英文\) ([如何下載](xref:index#how-to-download-a-sample))</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-590">[View or download sample code](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples) ([how to download](xref:index#how-to-download-a-sample))</span></span>

## <a name="routing-basics"></a><span data-ttu-id="f01e9-591">路由的基本概念</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-591">Routing basics</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-592">大部分應用程式都應該選擇基本的描述性路由傳送配置，讓 URL 可讀且有意義。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-592">Most apps should choose a basic and descriptive routing scheme so that URLs are readable and meaningful.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-593">預設慣例路由 `{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}`：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-593">The default conventional route `{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}`:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-594">支援基本的描述性路由配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-594">Supports a basic and descriptive routing scheme.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-595">適合作為 UI 型應用程式的起點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-595">Is a useful starting point for UI-based apps.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-596">在特殊情況下，開發人員通常會使用[屬性路由](xref:mvc/controllers/routing#attribute-routing)或專屬的慣例路由，新增額外的簡潔路由到應用程式的高流量區域 (例如，部落格和電子商務端點)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-596">Developers commonly add additional terse routes to high-traffic areas of an app in specialized situations (for example, blog and ecommerce endpoints) using [attribute routing](xref:mvc/controllers/routing#attribute-routing) or dedicated conventional routes.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-597">Web API 應該使用屬性路由傳送來將應用程式功能模型建構為作業由 HTTP 指令動詞代表的資源集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-597">Web APIs should use attribute routing to model the app's functionality as a set of resources where operations are represented by HTTP verbs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-598">這表示相同邏輯資源上的許多作業 (例如，GET、POST) 都會使用相同的 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-598">This means that many operations (for example, GET, POST) on the same logical resource will use the same URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-599">屬性路由提供仔細設計 API 公用端點配置所需的控制層級。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-599">Attribute routing provides a level of control that's needed to carefully design an API's public endpoint layout.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-600">Razor Pages 應用程式使用預設慣例路由，來提供應用程式 *Pages* 資料夾中的具名資源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-600">Razor Pages apps use default conventional routing to serve named resources in the *Pages* folder of an app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-601">還有其他慣例可讓您自訂 Razor Pages 路由行為。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-601">Additional conventions are available that allow you to customize Razor Pages routing behavior.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-602">如需詳細資訊，請參閱<xref:razor-pages/index>和<xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-602">For more information, see <xref:razor-pages/index> and <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-603">URL 產生支援允許在不需要硬式編碼的 URL 來連結應用程式的情況下開發應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-603">URL generation support allows the app to be developed without hard-coding URLs to link the app together.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-604">這項支援可讓您從基本路由設定開始，並在決定應用程式資源配置之後修改路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-604">This support allows for starting with a basic routing configuration and modifying the routes after the app's resource layout is determined.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-605">路由功能使用「端點」(`Endpoint`) 來表示應用程式中的邏輯端點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-605">Routing uses *endpoints* (`Endpoint`) to represent logical endpoints in an app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-606">端點會定義用來處理要求的一項委派及一個任意中繼資料集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-606">An endpoint defines a delegate to process requests and a collection of arbitrary metadata.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-607">中繼資料可根據附加至每個端點的原則和組態，來實作跨領域關注。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-607">The metadata is used implement cross-cutting concerns based on policies and configuration attached to each endpoint.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-608">路由系統具有下列特性：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-608">The routing system has the following characteristics:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-609">使用路由範本語法以 Token 化路由參數來定義路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-609">Route template syntax is used to define routes with tokenized route parameters.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-610">允許傳統式和屬性式端點組態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-610">Conventional-style and attribute-style endpoint configuration is permitted.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-611"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> 可用來判斷 URL 參數是否包含對指定端點條件約束有效的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-611"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> is used to determine whether a URL parameter contains a valid value for a given endpoint constraint.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-612">應用程式模型 (例如 MVC/Razor Pages) 會註冊其所有端點，這些端點的路由情節實作符合預期。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-612">App models, such as MVC/Razor Pages, register all of their endpoints, which have a predictable implementation of routing scenarios.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-613">路由實作會在中介軟體管線需要時制定路由決策。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-613">The routing implementation makes routing decisions wherever desired in the middleware pipeline.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-614">在路由中介軟體之後出現的中介軟體可以檢查指定要求 URI 的路由中介軟體端點決策。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-614">Middleware that appears after a Routing Middleware can inspect the result of the Routing Middleware's endpoint decision for a given request URI.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-615">您可以針對中介軟體管線中任何位置的應用程式，列舉其中的所有端點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-615">It's possible to enumerate all of the endpoints in the app anywhere in the middleware pipeline.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-616">應用程式可以根據端點資訊使用路由來產生 URL (例如，針對重新導向或連結)，因此避免硬式編碼的 URL，這有助於可維護性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-616">An app can use routing to generate URLs (for example, for redirection or links) based on endpoint information and thus avoid hard-coded URLs, which helps maintainability.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-617">URL 是根據支援任意擴充性的位址所產生：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-617">URL generation is based on addresses, which support arbitrary extensibility:</span></span>

  * <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-618">您可以在任何位置使用[相依性插入 (DI)](xref:fundamentals/dependency-injection) 來解析連結產生器 API (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator>)，以產生 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-618">The Link Generator API (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator>) can be resolved anywhere using [dependency injection (DI)](xref:fundamentals/dependency-injection) to generate URLs.</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-619">如果無法透過 DI 使用連結產生器 API，<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper> 會提供方法來建立 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-619">Where the Link Generator API isn't available via DI, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper> offers methods to build URLs.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-620">在 ASP.NET Core 2.2 中發行端點路由時，端點連結限制在 MVC/Razor Pages 動作和頁面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-620">With the release of endpoint routing in ASP.NET Core 2.2, endpoint linking is limited to MVC/Razor Pages actions and pages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-621">未來版本將規劃擴充端點連結功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-621">The expansions of endpoint-linking capabilities is planned for future releases.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-622">路由會透過 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RouterMiddleware> 類別連線到[中介軟體](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index)管線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-622">Routing is connected to the [middleware](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index) pipeline by the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RouterMiddleware> class.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-623">[ASP.NET Core MVC](xref:mvc/overview) 會將路由新增至中介軟體管線，作為其組態的一部分，並處理 MVC 和 Razor Pages 應用程式中的路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-623">[ASP.NET Core MVC](xref:mvc/overview) adds routing to the middleware pipeline as part of its configuration and handles routing in MVC and Razor Pages apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-624">若要了解如何使用路由作為獨立元件，請參閱[使用路由中介軟體](#use-routing-middleware)一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-624">To learn how to use routing as a standalone component, see the [Use Routing Middleware](#use-routing-middleware) section.</span></span>

### <a name="url-matching"></a><span data-ttu-id="f01e9-625">URL 比對</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-625">URL matching</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-626">URL 比對是路由用來將傳入要求分派給「端點」的處理序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-626">URL matching is the process by which routing dispatches an incoming request to an *endpoint*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-627">這個處理序是基於 URL 路徑中的資料，但是可以擴展為考慮要求中的任何資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-627">This process is based on data in the URL path but can be extended to consider any data in the request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-628">分派要求給不同處理常式的能力，是調整應用程式大小和複雜度的關鍵。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-628">The ability to dispatch requests to separate handlers is key to scaling the size and complexity of an app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-629">端點路由中的路由系統負責制定所有分派決策。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-629">The routing system in endpoint routing is responsible for all dispatching decisions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-630">由於中介軟體會根據所選取的端點來套用原則，因此請務必在路由系統內制定可能影響分派或應用安全性原則的任何決策。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-630">Since the middleware applies policies based on the selected endpoint, it's important that any decision that can affect dispatching or the application of security policies is made inside the routing system.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-631">執行端點委派時，會根據到目前為止所執行的要求處理，將 [RouteContext.RouteData](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.RouteData) 的屬性設定為適當的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-631">When the endpoint delegate is executed, the properties of [RouteContext.RouteData](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.RouteData) are set to appropriate values based on the request processing performed thus far.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-632">[RouteData.Values](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Values*) 是「路由值」的字典，而路由值產生自路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-632">[RouteData.Values](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Values*) is a dictionary of *route values* produced from the route.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-633">這些值通常是透過將 URL 語彙基元化來決定，可以用來接受使用者輸入，或在應用程式內做出進一步的分派決策。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-633">These values are usually determined by tokenizing the URL and can be used to accept user input or to make further dispatching decisions inside the app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-634">[RouteData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*) 是其他資料的屬性包，而這些資料與相符路由相關。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-634">[RouteData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*) is a property bag of additional data related to the matched route.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-635">提供了 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*> 來支援與每個路由建立關聯的狀態資料，因此應用程式可以依據符合哪一個路由來制定決策。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-635"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*> are provided to support associating state data with each route so that the app can make decisions based on which route matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-636">這些是開發人員定義的值，**不會**以任何方式影響路由的行為。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-636">These values are developer-defined and do **not** affect the behavior of routing in any way.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-637">此外，儲藏在 [RouteData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*) 中的值可以是任何類型，對比之下，[RouteData.Values](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Values) 則必須可轉換成字串或可從字串轉換。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-637">Additionally, values stashed in [RouteData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*) can be of any type, in contrast to [RouteData.Values](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Values), which must be convertible to and from strings.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-638">[RouteData.Routers](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers) 是成功符合要求的參與路由清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-638">[RouteData.Routers](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers) is a list of the routes that took part in successfully matching the request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-639">路由可以用巢狀方式置於彼此內部。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-639">Routes can be nested inside of one another.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-640"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> 屬性會透過導致產生相符項目的路由邏輯樹狀結構反映路徑。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-640">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> property reflects the path through the logical tree of routes that resulted in a match.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-641">一般而言，<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> 中的第一個項目是路由集合，應該用於產生 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-641">Generally, the first item in <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> is the route collection and should be used for URL generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-642"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> 中的最後一個項目是相符的路由處理常式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-642">The last item in <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> is the route handler that matched.</span></span>

<a name="lg"></a>

### <a name="url-generation-with-linkgenerator"></a><span data-ttu-id="f01e9-643">使用 LinkGenerator 產生 URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-643">URL generation with LinkGenerator</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-644">URL 產生是路由可用來依據一組路由值建立 URL 路徑的處理序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-644">URL generation is the process by which routing can create a URL path based on a set of route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-645">這可讓您在端點和存取它們的 URL 之間建立邏輯分隔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-645">This allows for a logical separation between your endpoints and the URLs that access them.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-646">端點路由包含連結產生器 API (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator>)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-646">Endpoint routing includes the Link Generator API (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator>).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-647"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> 是可從 DI 擷取的單一服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-647"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> is a singleton service that can be retrieved from DI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-648">您可以在執行要求內容外部使用此 API。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-648">The API can be used outside of the context of an executing request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-649">MVC 的 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper> 及依賴 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper> 的情節 (例如[標籤協助程式](xref:mvc/views/tag-helpers/intro)、HTML 協助程式和[動作結果](xref:mvc/controllers/actions)) 均使用連結產生器來提供連結產生功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-649">MVC's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper> and scenarios that rely on <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper>, such as [Tag Helpers](xref:mvc/views/tag-helpers/intro), HTML Helpers, and [Action Results](xref:mvc/controllers/actions), use the link generator to provide link generating capabilities.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-650">連結產生器背後支援的概念為「位址」和「位址配置」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-650">The link generator is backed by the concept of an *address* and *address schemes*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-651">位址配置可讓您判斷應考慮用於連結產生的端點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-651">An address scheme is a way of determining the endpoints that should be considered for link generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-652">例如，MVC/Razor Pages 中許多使用者所熟悉的路由名稱和路由值情節，都會實作為位址配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-652">For example, the route name and route values scenarios many users are familiar with from MVC/Razor Pages are implemented as an address scheme.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-653">連結產生器可以透過下列擴充方法，連結至 MVC/Razor Pages 動作和頁面：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-653">The link generator can link to MVC/Razor Pages actions and pages via the following extension methods:</span></span>

* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.ControllerLinkGeneratorExtensions.GetPathByAction*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.ControllerLinkGeneratorExtensions.GetUriByAction*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.PageLinkGeneratorExtensions.GetPathByPage*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.PageLinkGeneratorExtensions.GetUriByPage*>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-654">這些方法的多載接受包含 `HttpContext` 的引數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-654">An overload of these methods accepts arguments that include the `HttpContext`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-655">這些方法的功能等同於 `Url.Action` 和 `Url.Page`，但提供更多彈性和選項。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-655">These methods are functionally equivalent to `Url.Action` and `Url.Page` but offer additional flexibility and options.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-656">`GetPath*` 方法與 `Url.Action` 和 `Url.Page` 最類似，因為它們會產生包含絕對路徑的 URI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-656">The `GetPath*` methods are most similar to `Url.Action` and `Url.Page` in that they generate a URI containing an absolute path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-657">`GetUri*` 方法一律會產生包含配置和主機的絕對 URI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-657">The `GetUri*` methods always generate an absolute URI containing a scheme and host.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-658">接受 `HttpContext` 的方法會在執行要求的內容中產生 URI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-658">The methods that accept an `HttpContext` generate a URI in the context of the executing request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-659">除非遭到覆寫，否則會使用來自執行要求的環境路由值、URL 基底路徑、配置和主機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-659">The ambient route values, URL base path, scheme, and host from the executing request are used unless overridden.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-660">呼叫 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> 並指定一個位址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-660"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> is called with an address.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-661">執行下列兩個步驟來產生 URI：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-661">Generating a URI occurs in two steps:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-662">將位址繫結至符合該位址的端點清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-662">An address is bound to a list of endpoints that match the address.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-663">評估每個端點的 `RoutePattern`，直到找到符合所提供值的路由模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-663">Each endpoint's `RoutePattern` is evaluated until a route pattern that matches the supplied values is found.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-664">產生的輸出會與提供給連結產生器的其他 URI 組件合併並傳回。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-664">The resulting output is combined with the other URI parts supplied to the link generator and returned.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-665"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> 提供的方法支援適用於任何位址類型的標準連結產生功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-665">The methods provided by <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> support standard link generation capabilities for any type of address.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-666">使用連結產生器的最便利方式是透過執行特定位址類型作業的擴充方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-666">The most convenient way to use the link generator is through extension methods that perform operations for a specific address type.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-667">擴充方法</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-667">Extension Method</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-668">描述</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-668">Description</span></span>                                                         |
| ------------------ | ------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator.GetPathByAddress*> | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-669">根據提供的值產生具有絕對路徑的 URI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-669">Generates a URI with an absolute path based on the provided values.</span></span> |
| <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator.GetUriByAddress*> | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-670">根據提供的值產生絕對 URI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-670">Generates an absolute URI based on the provided values.</span></span>             |

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-671">注意呼叫 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> 方法的下列影響：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-671">Pay attention to the following implications of calling <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> methods:</span></span>
>
> * <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-672">使用 `GetUri*` 擴充方法，並注意應用程式組態不會驗證傳入要求的 `Host` 標頭。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-672">Use `GetUri*` extension methods with caution in an app configuration that doesn't validate the `Host` header of incoming requests.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-673">如果傳入要求的 `Host` 標頭未經驗證，則可能將未受信任的要求輸入傳回檢視/頁面 URI 中的用戶端。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-673">If the `Host` header of incoming requests isn't validated, untrusted request input can be sent back to the client in URIs in a view/page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-674">建議所有生產應用程式將其伺服器設定為驗證 `Host` 標頭是否為已知有效值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-674">We recommend that all production apps configure their server to validate the `Host` header against known valid values.</span></span>
>
> * <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-675">使用 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator>，並注意與 `Map` 或 `MapWhen` 搭配使用的中介軟體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-675">Use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> with caution in middleware in combination with `Map` or `MapWhen`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-676">`Map*` 會變更執行要求的基底路徑，這會影響連結產生的輸出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-676">`Map*` changes the base path of the executing request, which affects the output of link generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-677">所有的 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> API 都允許指定基底路徑。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-677">All of the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> APIs allow specifying a base path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-678">請一律指定空白基底路徑來恢復 `Map*` 對連結產生的影響。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-678">Always specify an empty base path to undo `Map*`'s affect on link generation.</span></span>

## <a name="differences-from-earlier-versions-of-routing"></a><span data-ttu-id="f01e9-679">與舊版路由的差異</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-679">Differences from earlier versions of routing</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-680">ASP.NET Core 2.2 或更新版本中的端點路由與 ASP.NET Core 中的舊版路由之間有一些差異：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-680">A few differences exist between endpoint routing in ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later and earlier versions of routing in ASP.NET Core:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-681">端點路由系統不支援以 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter> 為基礎的擴充性，包括從 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> 繼承。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-681">The endpoint routing system doesn't support <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>-based extensibility, including inheriting from <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-682">端點路由不支援 [WebApiCompatShim](https://www.nuget.org/packages/Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.WebApiCompatShim)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-682">Endpoint routing doesn't support [WebApiCompatShim](https://www.nuget.org/packages/Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.WebApiCompatShim).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-683">請使用 2.1 [相容性版本](xref:mvc/compatibility-version) (`.SetCompatibilityVersion(CompatibilityVersion.Version_2_1)`) 以繼續使用相容性填充碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-683">Use the 2.1 [compatibility version](xref:mvc/compatibility-version) (`.SetCompatibilityVersion(CompatibilityVersion.Version_2_1)`) to continue using the compatibility shim.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-684">端點路由與使用傳統路由時所產生 URI 大小寫的行為不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-684">Endpoint Routing has different behavior for the casing of generated URIs when using conventional routes.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-685">請考慮下列預設路由範本：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-685">Consider the following default route template:</span></span>

  ```csharp
  app.UseMvc(routes =>
  {
      routes.MapRoute("default", "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
  });
  ```

  <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-686">假設您使用下列路由來產生動作連結：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-686">Suppose you generate a link to an action using the following route:</span></span>

  ```csharp
  var link = Url.Action("ReadPost", "blog", new { id = 17, });
  ```

  <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-687">使用以 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter> 為基礎的路由，此程式碼會產生 `/blog/ReadPost/17` 的 URI，其遵守所提供路由值的大小寫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-687">With <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>-based routing, this code generates a URI of `/blog/ReadPost/17`, which respects the casing of the provided route value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-688">ASP.NET Core 2.2 或更新版本中的端點路由會產生 `/Blog/ReadPost/17` ("Blog" 為大寫)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-688">Endpoint routing in ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later produces `/Blog/ReadPost/17` ("Blog" is capitalized).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-689">端點路由提供 `IOutboundParameterTransformer` 介面，可用來全域自訂此行為，或為對應 URL 套用不同的慣例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-689">Endpoint routing provides the `IOutboundParameterTransformer` interface that can be used to customize this behavior globally or to apply different conventions for mapping URLs.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-690">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[參數轉換器參考](#parameter-transformer-reference)一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-690">For more information, see the [Parameter transformer reference](#parameter-transformer-reference) section.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-691">當嘗試連結至不存在的控制器/動作或頁面時，MVC/Razor Pages 所使用的連結產生與傳統路由的行為不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-691">Link Generation used by MVC/Razor Pages with conventional routes behaves differently when attempting to link to an controller/action or page that doesn't exist.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-692">請考慮下列預設路由範本：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-692">Consider the following default route template:</span></span>

  ```csharp
  app.UseMvc(routes =>
  {
  ```
