  ```csharp
      routes.MapRoute("default", "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
  });
  ```

  <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-693">假設您使用預設範本和下列程式碼來產生動作連結：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-693">Suppose you generate a link to an action using the default template with the following:</span></span>

  ```csharp
  var link = Url.Action("ReadPost", "Blog", new { id = 17, });
  ```

  <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-694">使用以 `IRouter` 為基礎的路由，結果一律為 `/Blog/ReadPost/17`，即使 `BlogController` 不存在或沒有 `ReadPost` 動作方法也一樣。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-694">With `IRouter`-based routing, the result is always `/Blog/ReadPost/17`, even if the `BlogController` doesn't exist or doesn't have a `ReadPost` action method.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-695">如預期，如果動作方法存在，則 ASP.NET Core 2.2 或更新版本中的端點路由會產生 `/Blog/ReadPost/17`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-695">As expected, endpoint routing in ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later produces `/Blog/ReadPost/17` if the action method exists.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-696">不過，如果動作不存在，則端點路由會產生空字串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-696">*However, endpoint routing produces an empty string if the action doesn't exist.*</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-697">就概念而言，如果動作不存在，則端點路由不會假設端點存在。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-697">Conceptually, endpoint routing doesn't assume that the endpoint exists if the action doesn't exist.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-698">連結產生「環境值失效演算法」在搭配端點路由使用時會有不同的行為。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-698">The link generation *ambient value invalidation algorithm* behaves differently when used with endpoint routing.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-699">「環境值失效」是一種演算法，會從目前執行的要求 (環境值) 決定可用於連結產生作業的路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-699">*Ambient value invalidation* is the algorithm that decides which route values from the currently executing request (the ambient values) can be used in link generation operations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-700">傳統路由一律會在連結至其他動作時，使額外的路由值失效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-700">Conventional routing always invalidated extra route values when linking to a different action.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-701">在 ASP.NET Core 2.2 版以前，屬性路由沒有此行為。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-701">Attribute routing didn't have this behavior prior to the release of ASP.NET Core 2.2.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-702">在舊版的 ASP.NET Core 中，連結至使用相同路由參數名稱的其他動作會導致連結產生錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-702">In earlier versions of ASP.NET Core, links to another action that use the same route parameter names resulted in link generation errors.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-703">在 ASP.NET Core 2.2 或更新版本中，這兩種路由形式都會在連結至其他動作時使值失效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-703">In ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later, both forms of routing invalidate values when linking to another action.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-704">請考慮 ASP.NET Core 2.1 或更舊版本中的下列範例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-704">Consider the following example in ASP.NET Core 2.1 or earlier.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-705">連結至其他動作 (或其他頁面) 時，路由值可能會不適當地重複使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-705">When linking to another action (or another page), route values can be reused in undesirable ways.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-706">在 */Pages/Store/Product.cshtml* 中：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-706">In */Pages/Store/Product.cshtml*:</span></span>

  ```cshtml
  @page "{id}"
  @Url.Page("/Login")
  ```

  <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-707">在 */Pages/Login.cshtml* 中：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-707">In */Pages/Login.cshtml*:</span></span>

  ```cshtml
  @page "{id?}"
  ```

  <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-708">如果 URI 在 ASP.NET Core 2.1 或更舊版本中為 `/Store/Product/18`，則 `@Url.Page("/Login")` 在 Store/Info 頁面中產生的連結為 `/Login/18`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-708">If the URI is `/Store/Product/18` in ASP.NET Core 2.1 or earlier, the link generated on the Store/Info page by `@Url.Page("/Login")` is `/Login/18`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-709">這會重複使用 `id` 值 18，即使連結目的地是完全不同的應用程式組件也一樣。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-709">The `id` value of 18 is reused, even though the link destination is different part of the app entirely.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-710">`/Login` 頁面內容中的 `id` 路由值可能是使用者識別碼值，而不是市集產品識別碼值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-710">The `id` route value in the context of the `/Login` page is probably a user ID value, not a store product ID value.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-711">在 ASP.NET Core 2.2 或更新版本中的端點路由中，結果為 `/Login`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-711">In endpoint routing with ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later, the result is `/Login`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-712">當連結的目的地是不同的動作或頁面時，不會重複使用環境值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-712">Ambient values aren't reused when the linked destination is a different action or page.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-713">往返路由參數語法：使用雙星號 (`**`) catch-all 參數語法時，斜線不會經過編碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-713">Round-tripping route parameter syntax: Forward slashes aren't encoded when using a double-asterisk (`**`) catch-all parameter syntax.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-714">在連結產生期間，除了斜線，路由系統還會對雙星號 (`**`) catch-all 參數 (例如 `{**myparametername}`) 中擷取的值進行編碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-714">During link generation, the routing system encodes the value captured in a double-asterisk (`**`) catch-all parameter (for example, `{**myparametername}`) except the forward slashes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-715">ASP.NET Core 2.2 或更新版本中以 `IRouter` 為基礎的路由支援雙星號 catch-all。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-715">The double-asterisk catch-all is supported with `IRouter`-based routing in ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-716">舊版 ASP.NET Core 中的單一星號 catch-all (`{*myparametername}`) 參數語法仍會受到支援，而且斜線會經過編碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-716">The single asterisk catch-all parameter syntax in prior versions of ASP.NET Core (`{*myparametername}`) remains supported, and forward slashes are encoded.</span></span>

  | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-717">路由</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-717">Route</span></span>              | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-718">以下列項目產生的連結：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-718">Link generated with</span></span><br>`Url.Action(new { category = "admin/products" })`&hellip; |
  | ------------------ | --------------------------------------------------------------------- |
  | `/search/{*page}`  | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-719">`/search/admin%2Fproducts` (斜線會經過編碼)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-719">`/search/admin%2Fproducts` (the forward slash is encoded)</span></span>             |
  | `/search/{**page}` | `/search/admin/products`                                              |

### <a name="middleware-example"></a><span data-ttu-id="f01e9-720">中介軟體範例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-720">Middleware example</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-721">在下列範例中，中介軟體使用 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> API 建立列出市集產品的動作方法連結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-721">In the following example, a middleware uses the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> API to create link to an action method that lists store products.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-722">應用程式中的任何類別都可以使用連結產生器，方法是將它插入類別並呼叫 `GenerateLink`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-722">Using the link generator by injecting it into a class and calling `GenerateLink` is available to any class in an app.</span></span>

```csharp
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing;

public class ProductsLinkMiddleware
{
    private readonly LinkGenerator _linkGenerator;

    public ProductsLinkMiddleware(RequestDelegate next, LinkGenerator linkGenerator)
    {
        _linkGenerator = linkGenerator;
    }

    public async Task InvokeAsync(HttpContext httpContext)
    {
        var url = _linkGenerator.GetPathByAction("ListProducts", "Store");

        httpContext.Response.ContentType = "text/plain";

        await httpContext.Response.WriteAsync($"Go to {url} to see our products.");
    }
}
```

### <a name="create-routes"></a><span data-ttu-id="f01e9-723">建立路由</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-723">Create routes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-724">大部分的應用程式會藉由呼叫 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> 或其中一個 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteBuilder> 上定義的類似擴充方法來定建立路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-724">Most apps create routes by calling <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> or one of the similar extension methods defined on <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteBuilder>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-725">任何 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteBuilder> 擴充方法都會建立 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> 的執行個體，並將它新增至路由集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-725">Any of the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteBuilder> extension methods create an instance of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> and add it to the route collection.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-726"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> 不接受路由處理常式參數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-726"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> doesn't accept a route handler parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-727"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> 只會新增 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder.DefaultHandler*> 所處理的路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-727"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> only adds routes that are handled by the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder.DefaultHandler*>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-728">若要深入了解 MVC 中的路由功能，請參閱 <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-728">To learn more about routing in MVC, see <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-729">下列程式碼範例是典型 ASP.NET Core MVC 路由定義所使用的 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> 呼叫範例：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-729">The following code example is an example of a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> call used by a typical ASP.NET Core MVC route definition:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-730">此範本會比對 URL 路徑，並擷取路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-730">This template matches a URL path and extracts the route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-731">例如，路徑 `/Products/Details/17` 會產生下列路由值：`{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 17 }`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-731">For example, the path `/Products/Details/17` generates the following route values: `{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 17 }`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-732">路由值是透過將 URL 路徑分割成區段，並比對每個區段與路由範本中的「路由參數」名稱來判定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-732">Route values are determined by splitting the URL path into segments and matching each segment with the *route parameter* name in the route template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-733">路由參數為具名。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-733">Route parameters are named.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-734">參數是透過以括弧 `{ ... }` 括住參數名稱來定義。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-734">The parameters defined by enclosing the parameter name in braces `{ ... }`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-735">上述範本也可以比對 URL 路徑 `/` 並產生值 `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-735">The preceding template could also match the URL path `/` and produce the values `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-736">發生這種情況是因為 `{controller}` 和 `{action}` 路由參數有預設值，而 `id` 路由參數為選擇性參數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-736">This occurs because the `{controller}` and `{action}` route parameters have default values and the `id` route parameter is optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-737">路由參數名稱之後緊接著值的等號 (`=`) 會定義參數預設值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-737">An equals sign (`=`) followed by a value after the route parameter name defines a default value for the parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-738">路由參數名稱之後的問號 (`?`) 會定義選擇性參數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-738">A question mark (`?`) after the route parameter name defines an optional parameter.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-739">在路由相符時，具有預設值的路由參數一定會產生路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-739">Route parameters with a default value *always* produce a route value when the route matches.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-740">如果沒有任何對應的 URL 路徑區段，選擇性參數不會產生路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-740">Optional parameters don't produce a route value if there was no corresponding URL path segment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-741">如需路由範本情節和語法的詳細描述，請參閱[路由範本參考](#route-template-reference)一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-741">See the [Route template reference](#route-template-reference) section for a thorough description of route template scenarios and syntax.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-742">在下列範例中，路由參數定義 `{id:int}` 會定義 `id` 路由參數的[路由條件約束](#route-constraint-reference)：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-742">In the following example, the route parameter definition `{id:int}` defines a [route constraint](#route-constraint-reference) for the `id` route parameter:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id:int}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-743">此範本會符合 `/Products/Details/17` 等 URL 路徑，但不符合 `/Products/Details/Apples`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-743">This template matches a URL path like `/Products/Details/17` but not `/Products/Details/Apples`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-744">路由條件約束會實作 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>，並檢查路由值以進行驗證。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-744">Route constraints implement <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> and inspect route values to verify them.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-745">在此範例中，路由值 `id` 必須可以轉換為整數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-745">In this example, the route value `id` must be convertible to an integer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-746">如需架構所提供之路由條件約束的說明，請參閱[路由條件約束參考](#route-constraint-reference)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-746">See [route-constraint-reference](#route-constraint-reference) for an explanation of route constraints provided by the framework.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-747"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> 的其他多載接受 `constraints`、`dataTokens` 和 `defaults` 的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-747">Additional overloads of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> accept values for `constraints`, `dataTokens`, and `defaults`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-748">這些參數通常是用來傳遞匿名類型的物件，其中匿名類型的屬性名稱符合路由參數名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-748">The typical usage of these parameters is to pass an anonymously typed object, where the property names of the anonymous type match route parameter names.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-749">下列 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> 範例會建立對等的路由：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-749">The following <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> examples create equivalent routes:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default_route",
    template: "{controller}/{action}/{id?}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Home", action = "Index" });

routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default_route",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
```

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-750">對於簡單的路由而言，定義條件約束和預設的內嵌語法可能很方便。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-750">The inline syntax for defining constraints and defaults can be convenient for simple routes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-751">不過，內嵌語法不支援某些情節 (例如資料語彙基元)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-751">However, there are scenarios, such as data tokens, that aren't supported by inline syntax.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-752">下列範例將示範一些其他情節：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-752">The following example demonstrates a few additional scenarios:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "blog",
    template: "Blog/{**article}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Blog", action = "ReadArticle" });
```

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-753">上述範本會比對 `/Blog/All-About-Routing/Introduction` 等 URL 路徑，並擷取值 `{ controller = Blog, action = ReadArticle, article = All-About-Routing/Introduction }`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-753">The preceding template matches a URL path like `/Blog/All-About-Routing/Introduction` and extracts the values `{ controller = Blog, action = ReadArticle, article = All-About-Routing/Introduction }`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-754">即使範本中沒有任何對應的路由參數，路由也會產生 `controller` 和 `action` 的預設路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-754">The default route values for `controller` and `action` are produced by the route even though there are no corresponding route parameters in the template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-755">預設值可以在路由範本中指定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-755">Default values can be specified in the route template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-756">`article` 路由參數透過在路由參數名稱之前加上雙星號 (`**`) 來定義為 *catch-all*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-756">The `article` route parameter is defined as a *catch-all* by the appearance of an double asterisk (`**`) before the route parameter name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-757">全部擷取路由參數會擷取 URL 路徑的其餘部分，而且也可以符合空字串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-757">Catch-all route parameters capture the remainder of the URL path and can also match the empty string.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-758">下列範例會新增路由條件約束和資料語彙基元：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-758">The following example adds route constraints and data tokens:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "us_english_products",
    template: "en-US/Products/{id}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Products", action = "Details" },
    constraints: new { id = new IntRouteConstraint() },
    dataTokens: new { locale = "en-US" });
```

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-759">上述範本會比對 `/en-US/Products/5` 等 URL 路徑，並擷取值 `{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 5 }` 和資料語彙基元 `{ locale = en-US }`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-759">The preceding template matches a URL path like `/en-US/Products/5` and extracts the values `{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 5 }` and the data tokens `{ locale = en-US }`.</span></span>

![[區域變數] 視窗語彙基元](routing/_static/tokens.png)

### <a name="route-class-url-generation"></a><span data-ttu-id="f01e9-761">路由類別 URL 產生</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-761">Route class URL generation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-762"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> 類別也可以結合一組路由值與其路由範本來產生 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-762">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> class can also perform URL generation by combining a set of route values with its route template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-763">這在邏輯上是比對 URL 路徑的反向處理序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-763">This is logically the reverse process of matching the URL path.</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-764">若要進一步了解 URL 產生，請假設您想要產生的 URL，並考慮路由範本將會如何比對該 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-764">To better understand URL generation, imagine what URL you want to generate and then think about how a route template would match that URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-765">產生的值為何？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-765">What values would be produced?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-766">這與 URL 產生在 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> 類別中的運作方式大致相同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-766">This is the rough equivalent of how URL generation works in the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> class.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-767">下列範例使用一般 ASP.NET Core MVC 預設路由：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-767">The following example uses a general ASP.NET Core MVC default route:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-768">路由值為 `{ controller = Products, action = List }` 時，會產生 URL `/Products/List`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-768">With the route values `{ controller = Products, action = List }`, the URL `/Products/List` is generated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-769">路由值會取代對應的路由參數，以形成 URL 路徑。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-769">The route values are substituted for the corresponding route parameters to form the URL path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-770">由於 `id` 是選擇性路由參數，因此沒有 `id` 值也可以成功產生 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-770">Since `id` is an optional route parameter, the URL is successfully generated without a value for `id`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-771">路由值為 `{ controller = Home, action = Index }` 時，會產生 URL `/`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-771">With the route values `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`, the URL `/` is generated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-772">所提供的路由值符合預設值，因此可以放心地省略這些預設值對應的區段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-772">The provided route values match the default values, and the segments corresponding to the default values are safely omitted.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-773">這兩個產生的 URL 會使用下列路由定義 (`/Home/Index` 和 `/`) 反覆存取，並產生用來產生 URL 的相同路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-773">Both URLs generated round-trip with the following route definition (`/Home/Index` and `/`) produce the same route values that were used to generate the URL.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-774">使用 ASP.NET Core MVC 的應用程式應該使用 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.Routing.UrlHelper> 來產生 URL，而不是直接呼叫路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-774">An app using ASP.NET Core MVC should use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.Routing.UrlHelper> to generate URLs instead of calling into routing directly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-775">如需 URL 產生的詳細資訊，請參閱 [URI 產生參考](#url-generation-reference)一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-775">For more information on URL generation, see the [Url generation reference](#url-generation-reference) section.</span></span>

## <a name="use-routing-middleware"></a><span data-ttu-id="f01e9-776">使用路由中介軟體</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-776">Use Routing Middleware</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-777">參考應用程式專案檔中的 [Microsoft.AspNetCore.App 中繼套件](xref:fundamentals/metapackage-app)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-777">Reference the [Microsoft.AspNetCore.App metapackage](xref:fundamentals/metapackage-app) in the app's project file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-778">在 `Startup.ConfigureServices` 中，將路由新增至服務容器：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-778">Add routing to the service container in `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/2.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_ConfigureServices&highlight=3)]

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-779">路由必須設定在 `Startup.Configure` 方法中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-779">Routes must be configured in the `Startup.Configure` method.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-780">範例應用程式使用下列 API：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-780">The sample app uses the following APIs:</span></span>

* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder>
* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-781"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> &ndash; 僅符合 HTTP GET 要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-781"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> &ndash; Matches only HTTP GET requests.</span></span>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RoutingBuilderExtensions.UseRouter*>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/2.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_RouteHandler)]

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-782">下表顯示使用指定 URL 的回應。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-782">The following table shows the responses with the given URIs.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-783">URI</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-783">URI</span></span>                    | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-784">回應</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-784">Response</span></span>                                          |
| ---------------------- | ------------------------------------------------- |
| `/package/create/3`    | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-785">Hello!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-785">Hello!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-786">Route values: [operation, create], [id, 3]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-786">Route values: [operation, create], [id, 3]</span></span> |
| `/package/track/-3`    | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-787">Hello!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-787">Hello!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-788">Route values: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-788">Route values: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span></span> |
| `/package/track/-3/`   | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-789">Hello!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-789">Hello!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-790">Route values: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-790">Route values: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span></span> |
| `/package/track/`      | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-791">要求失敗，沒有相符項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-791">The request falls through, no match.</span></span>              |
| `GET /hello/Joe`       | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-792">Hi, Joe!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-792">Hi, Joe!</span></span>                                          |
| `POST /hello/Joe`      | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-793">要求失敗，僅符合 HTTP GET。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-793">The request falls through, matches HTTP GET only.</span></span> |
| `GET /hello/Joe/Smith` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-794">要求失敗，沒有相符項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-794">The request falls through, no match.</span></span>              |

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-795">架構會提供一組擴充方法來建立路由 (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions>)：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-795">The framework provides a set of extension methods for creating routes (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions>):</span></span>

* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapDelete*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareDelete*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareGet*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewarePost*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewarePut*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareRoute*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareVerb*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPost*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPut*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapVerb*>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-796">`Map[Verb]` 方法會使用條件約束，將路由限制為方法名稱中的 HTTP 指令動詞。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-796">The `Map[Verb]` methods use constraints to limit the route to the HTTP Verb in the method name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-797">如需範例，請參閱 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> 與 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapVerb*>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-797">For example, see <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> and <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapVerb*>.</span></span>

## <a name="route-template-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="f01e9-798">路由範本參考</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-798">Route template reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-799">大括弧 (`{ ... }`) 內的語彙基元定義路由相符時會繫結的「路由參數」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-799">Tokens within curly braces (`{ ... }`) define *route parameters* that are bound if the route is matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-800">您可以在路由區段中定義多個路由參數，但其必須以常值分隔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-800">You can define more than one route parameter in a route segment, but they must be separated by a literal value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-801">例如，`{controller=Home}{action=Index}` 不是有效的路由，因為 `{controller}` 與 `{action}` 之間沒有任何常值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-801">For example, `{controller=Home}{action=Index}` isn't a valid route, since there's no literal value between `{controller}` and `{action}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-802">這些路由參數必須有一個名稱，並且可以指定其他屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-802">These route parameters must have a name and may have additional attributes specified.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-803">路由參數之外的常值文字 (例如，`{id}`) 和路徑分隔符號 `/` 必須符合 URL 中的文字。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-803">Literal text other than route parameters (for example, `{id}`) and the path separator `/` must match the text in the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-804">文字比對會區分大小寫，並以 URL 路徑的已解碼表示法為基礎。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-804">Text matching is case-insensitive and based on the decoded representation of the URLs path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-805">若要比對常值路由參數分隔符號 (`{` 或 `}`)，請重複字元 (`{{` 或 `}}`) 來將分隔符號逸出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-805">To match a literal route parameter delimiter (`{` or `}`), escape the delimiter by repeating the character (`{{` or `}}`).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-806">URL 模式嘗試擷取具有選擇性副檔名的檔案名稱時，具有其他考量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-806">URL patterns that attempt to capture a file name with an optional file extension have additional considerations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-807">以範本 `files/{filename}.{ext?}` 為例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-807">For example, consider the template `files/{filename}.{ext?}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-808">當 `filename` 和 `ext` 都存在值時，就會填入這兩個值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-808">When values for both `filename` and `ext` exist, both values are populated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-809">如果 URL 中只有 `filename` 存在值，由於結尾的句點 (`.`) 是選擇性項目，因此路由相符。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-809">If only a value for `filename` exists in the URL, the route matches because the trailing period (`.`) is  optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-810">下列 URL 符合此路由：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-810">The following URLs match this route:</span></span>

* `/files/myFile.txt`
* `/files/myFile`

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-811">您可以使用一個星號 (`*`) 或雙星號 (`**`) 作為路由參數的前置詞，以繫結至 URI 的其餘部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-811">You can use an asterisk (`*`) or double asterisk (`**`) as a prefix to a route parameter to bind to the rest of the URI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-812">這稱為 *catch-all* 參數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-812">These are called a *catch-all* parameters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-813">例如，`blog/{**slug}` 符合以 `/blog` 開頭且其後有任何值 (這會指派給 `slug` 路由值) 的所有 URI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-813">For example, `blog/{**slug}` matches any URI that starts with `/blog` and has any value following it, which is assigned to the `slug` route value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-814">全部擷取參數也可以符合空字串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-814">Catch-all parameters can also match the empty string.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-815">當使用路由產生 URL (包括路徑分隔符號 (`/`) 字元) 時，catch-all 參數會逸出適當的字元。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-815">The catch-all parameter escapes the appropriate characters when the route is used to generate a URL, including path separator (`/`) characters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-816">例如，路由值為 `{ path = "my/path" }` 的路由 `foo/{*path}` 會產生 `foo/my%2Fpath`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-816">For example, the route `foo/{*path}` with route values `{ path = "my/path" }` generates `foo/my%2Fpath`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-817">請注意逸出的斜線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-817">Note the escaped forward slash.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-818">若要反覆存取路徑分隔符號字元，請使用 `**` 路由參數前置詞。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-818">To round-trip path separator characters, use the `**` route parameter prefix.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-819">具有 `{ path = "my/path" }` 的路由 `foo/{**path}` 會產生 `foo/my/path`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-819">The route `foo/{**path}` with `{ path = "my/path" }` generates `foo/my/path`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-820">路由參數可能有「預設值」，指定方法是在參數名稱之後指定預設值，並以等號 (`=`) 分隔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-820">Route parameters may have *default values* designated by specifying the default value after the parameter name separated by an equals sign (`=`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-821">例如，`{controller=Home}` 定義 `Home` 作為 `controller` 的預設值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-821">For example, `{controller=Home}` defines `Home` as the default value for `controller`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-822">如果 URL 中沒有用於參數的任何值，則會使用預設值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-822">The default value is used if no value is present in the URL for the parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-823">路由參數也可以設為選擇性，方法是在參數名稱結尾附加問號 (`?`)，如 `id?` 中所示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-823">Route parameters are made optional by appending a question mark (`?`) to the end of the parameter name, as in `id?`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-824">選擇性值與預設路由參數之間的差異在於，具有預設值的路由參數一定會產生值&mdash;選擇性參數只有在要求 URL 提供值時才會有值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-824">The difference between optional values and default route parameters is that a route parameter with a default value always produces a value&mdash;an optional parameter has a value only when a value is provided by the request URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-825">路由參數可能具有條件約束，這些條件約束必須符合與 URL 繫結的路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-825">Route parameters may have constraints that must match the route value bound from the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-826">在路由參數名稱之後新增分號 (`:`) 和條件約束名稱，即可指定路由參數的「內嵌條件約束」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-826">Adding a colon (`:`) and constraint name after the route parameter name specifies an *inline constraint* on a route parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-827">如果條件約束需要引數，這些引數會在條件約束名稱後面以括弧 (`(...)`) 括住。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-827">If the constraint requires arguments, they're enclosed in parentheses (`(...)`) after the constraint name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-828">指定多個內嵌條件約束的方法是附加另一個冒號 (`:`) 和條件約束名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-828">Multiple inline constraints can be specified by appending another colon (`:`) and constraint name.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-829">條件約束名稱和引述會傳遞至 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IInlineConstraintResolver> 服務來建立 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> 的執行個體，以用於 URL 處理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-829">The constraint name and arguments are passed to the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IInlineConstraintResolver> service to create an instance of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> to use in URL processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-830">例如，路由範本 `blog/{article:minlength(10)}` 指定具有引數 `10` 的 `minlength` 條件約束。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-830">For example, the route template `blog/{article:minlength(10)}` specifies a `minlength` constraint with the argument `10`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-831">如需路由條件約束詳細資訊和架構所提供的條件約束清單，請參閱[路由條件約束參考](#route-constraint-reference)一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-831">For more information on route constraints and a list of the constraints provided by the framework, see the [Route constraint reference](#route-constraint-reference) section.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-832">路由參數也可以具有參數轉換器，以在產生連結及根據 URL 比對動作和頁面時，轉換參數的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-832">Route parameters may also have parameter transformers, which transform a parameter's value when generating links and matching actions and pages to URLs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-833">與條件約束類似，可以透過在路徑參數名稱後面新增冒號 (`:`) 和轉換器名稱，將參數轉換器內嵌新增至路徑參數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-833">Like constraints, parameter transformers can be added inline to a route parameter by adding a colon (`:`) and transformer name after the route parameter name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-834">例如，路由範本 `blog/{article:slugify}` 會指定 `slugify` 轉換器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-834">For example, the route template `blog/{article:slugify}` specifies a `slugify` transformer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-835">如需參數轉換器的詳細資訊，請參閱[參數轉器參考](#parameter-transformer-reference)一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-835">For more information on parameter transformers, see the [Parameter transformer reference](#parameter-transformer-reference) section.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-836">下表示範範例路由範本及其行為。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-836">The following table demonstrates example route templates and their behavior.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-837">路由範本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-837">Route Template</span></span>                           | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-838">範例比對 URI</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-838">Example Matching URI</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-839">要求 URI&hellip;</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-839">The request URI&hellip;</span></span>                                                    |
| ---------------------------------------- | ----------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `hello`                                  | `/hello`                | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-840">只比對單一路徑 `/hello`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-840">Only matches the single path `/hello`.</span></span>                                     |
| `{Page=Home}`                            | `/`                     | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-841">比對並將 `Page` 設定為 `Home`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-841">Matches and sets `Page` to `Home`.</span></span>                                         |
| `{Page=Home}`                            | `/Contact`              | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-842">比對並將 `Page` 設定為 `Contact`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-842">Matches and sets `Page` to `Contact`.</span></span>                                      |
| `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`            | `/Products/List`        | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-843">對應至 `Products` 控制器和 `List` 動作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-843">Maps to the `Products` controller and `List` action.</span></span>                       |
| `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`            | `/Products/Details/123` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-844">對應至 `Products` 控制器和 `Details` 動作 (`id` 設定為 123)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-844">Maps to the `Products` controller and  `Details` action (`id` set to 123).</span></span> |
| `{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}` | `/`                     | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-845">對應至 `Home` 控制器和 `Index` 方法 (會忽略 `id`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-845">Maps to the `Home` controller and `Index` method (`id` is ignored).</span></span>        |

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-846">使用範本通常是最簡單的路由方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-846">Using a template is generally the simplest approach to routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-847">條件約束和預設值也可以在路由範本外部指定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-847">Constraints and defaults can also be specified outside the route template.</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-848">啟用[記錄](xref:fundamentals/logging/index)以查看內建路由實作 (例如 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>) 如何符合要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-848">Enable [Logging](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) to see how the built-in routing implementations, such as <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>, match requests.</span></span>

## <a name="reserved-routing-names"></a><span data-ttu-id="f01e9-849">保留的路由名稱</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-849">Reserved routing names</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-850">下列關鍵字是保留的名稱，不能用作路由名稱或參數：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-850">The following keywords are reserved names and can't be used as route names or parameters:</span></span>

* `action`
* `area`
* `controller`
* `handler`
* `page`

## <a name="route-constraint-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="f01e9-851">路由條件約束參考</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-851">Route constraint reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-852">路由條件約束執行時機是出現符合傳入 URL 的項目，並將 URL 路徑語彙基元化成路由值時。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-852">Route constraints execute when a match has occurred to the incoming URL and the URL path is tokenized into route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-853">路由條件約束通常會透過路由範本檢查相關聯的路由值，並對是否可接受值做出是/否決策。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-853">Route constraints generally inspect the route value associated via the route template and make a yes/no decision about whether or not the value is acceptable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-854">某些路由條件約束會使用路由值以外的資料，以考慮是否可以路由要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-854">Some route constraints use data outside the route value to consider whether the request can be routed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-855">例如，<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Constraints.HttpMethodRouteConstraint> 可以依據其 HTTP 指令動詞接受或拒絕要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-855">For example, the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Constraints.HttpMethodRouteConstraint> can accept or reject a request based on its HTTP verb.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-856">條件約束可用於路由要求和連結產生。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-856">Constraints are used in routing requests and link generation.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-857">請勿針對**輸入驗證**使用條件約束。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-857">Don't use constraints for **input validation**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-858">如果針對**輸入驗證**使用條件約束，則無效的輸入會導致產生「404 - 找不到」回應，而不是「400 - 錯誤要求」與適當的錯誤訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-858">If constraints are used for **input validation**, invalid input results in a *404 - Not Found* response instead of a *400 - Bad Request* with an appropriate error message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-859">路由條件約束會用來**釐清**類似的路由，而不是用來驗證特定路由的輸入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-859">Route constraints are used to **disambiguate** similar routes, not to validate the inputs for a particular route.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-860">下表示範範例路由條件約束及其預期行為。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-860">The following table demonstrates example route constraints and their expected behavior.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-861">條件約束</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-861">constraint</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-862">範例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-862">Example</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-863">範例相符項目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-863">Example Matches</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-864">注意事項</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-864">Notes</span></span> |
| ---------- | ------- | --------------- | ----- |
| `int` | `{id:int}` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-865">`123456789`、 `-123456789`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-865">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-866">符合任何整數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-866">Matches any integer</span></span> |
| `bool` | `{active:bool}` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-867">`true`、 `FALSE`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-867">`true`, `FALSE`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-868">符合 `true` 或 `false` (不區分大小寫)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-868">Matches `true` or `false` (case-insensitive)</span></span> |
| `datetime` | `{dob:datetime}` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-869">`2016-12-31`、 `2016-12-31 7:32pm`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-869">`2016-12-31`, `2016-12-31 7:32pm`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-870">符合有效的 `DateTime` 值 (在不因國別而異的文化特性中 - 請參閱警告)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-870">Matches a valid `DateTime` value (in the invariant culture - see warning)</span></span> |
| `decimal` | `{price:decimal}` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-871">`49.99`、 `-1,000.01`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-871">`49.99`, `-1,000.01`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-872">符合有效的 `decimal` 值 (在不因國別而異的文化特性中 - 請參閱警告)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-872">Matches a valid `decimal` value (in the invariant culture - see warning)</span></span> |
| `double` | `{weight:double}` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-873">`1.234`、 `-1,001.01e8`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-873">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-874">符合有效的 `double` 值 (在不因國別而異的文化特性中 - 請參閱警告)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-874">Matches a valid `double` value (in the invariant culture - see warning)</span></span> |
| `float` | `{weight:float}` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-875">`1.234`、 `-1,001.01e8`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-875">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-876">符合有效的 `float` 值 (在不因國別而異的文化特性中 - 請參閱警告)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-876">Matches a valid `float` value (in the invariant culture - see warning)</span></span> |
| `guid` | `{id:guid}` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-877">`CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638`、 `{CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638}`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-877">`CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638`, `{CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638}`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-878">符合有效的 `Guid` 值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-878">Matches a valid `Guid` value</span></span> |
| `long` | `{ticks:long}` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-879">`123456789`、 `-123456789`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-879">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-880">符合有效的 `long` 值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-880">Matches a valid `long` value</span></span> |
| `minlength(value)` | `{username:minlength(4)}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-881">字串必須至少有 4 個字元</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-881">String must be at least 4 characters</span></span> |
| `maxlength(value)` | `{filename:maxlength(8)}` | `Richard` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-882">字串不能超過 8 個字元</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-882">String must be no more than 8 characters</span></span> |
| `length(length)` | `{filename:length(12)}` | `somefile.txt` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-883">字串長度必須剛好是 12 個字元</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-883">String must be exactly 12 characters long</span></span> |
| `length(min,max)` | `{filename:length(8,16)}` | `somefile.txt` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-884">字串長度必須至少有 8 個字元，但不能超過 16 個字元</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-884">String must be at least 8 and no more than 16 characters long</span></span> |
| `min(value)` | `{age:min(18)}` | `19` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-885">整數值必須至少為 18</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-885">Integer value must be at least 18</span></span> |
| `max(value)` | `{age:max(120)}` | `91` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-886">整數值不能超過 120</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-886">Integer value must be no more than 120</span></span> |
| `range(min,max)` | `{age:range(18,120)}` | `91` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-887">整數值必須至少為 18，但不能超過 120</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-887">Integer value must be at least 18 but no more than 120</span></span> |
| `alpha` | `{name:alpha}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-888">字串必須包含一或多個字母字元 (`a`-`z`，不區分大小寫)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-888">String must consist of one or more alphabetical characters (`a`-`z`, case-insensitive)</span></span> |
| `regex(expression)` | `{ssn:regex(^\\d{{3}}-\\d{{2}}-\\d{{4}}$)}` | `123-45-6789` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-889">字串必須符合規則運算式 (請參閱有關定義規則運算式的提示)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-889">String must match the regular expression (see tips about defining a regular expression)</span></span> |
| `required` | `{name:required}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-890">用來強制執行在 URL 產生期間呈現非參數值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-890">Used to enforce that a non-parameter value is present during URL generation</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-891">以冒號分隔的多個條件約束，可以套用至單一參數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-891">Multiple, colon-delimited constraints can be applied to a single parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-892">例如，下列條件約束會將參數限制在 1 或更大的整數值：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-892">For example, the following constraint restricts a parameter to an integer value of 1 or greater:</span></span>

```csharp
[Route("users/{id:int:min(1)}")]
public User GetUserById(int id) { }
```

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-893">確認 URL 可以轉換成 CLR 類型的路由條件約束 (例如 `int` 或 `DateTime`) 一律使用不因國別而異的文化特性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-893">Route constraints that verify the URL and are converted to a CLR type (such as `int` or `DateTime`) always use the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-894">這些條件約束假設 URL 不可當地語系化。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-894">These constraints assume that the URL is non-localizable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-895">架構提供的路由條件約束不會修改路由值中儲存的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-895">The framework-provided route constraints don't modify the values stored in route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-896">所有從 URL 剖析而來的路由值會儲存為字串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-896">All route values parsed from the URL are stored as strings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-897">例如，`float` 條件約束會嘗試將路由值轉換成浮點數，但轉換的值只能用來確認它可以轉換成浮點數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-897">For example, the `float` constraint attempts to convert the route value to a float, but the converted value is used only to verify it can be converted to a float.</span></span>

## <a name="regular-expressions"></a><span data-ttu-id="f01e9-898">規則運算式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-898">Regular expressions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-899">ASP.NET Core 架構將 `RegexOptions.IgnoreCase | RegexOptions.Compiled | RegexOptions.CultureInvariant` 新增至規則運算式建構函式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-899">The ASP.NET Core framework adds `RegexOptions.IgnoreCase | RegexOptions.Compiled | RegexOptions.CultureInvariant` to the regular expression constructor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-900">如需這些成員的說明，請參閱 <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.RegexOptions>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-900">See <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.RegexOptions> for a description of these members.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-901">規則運算式使用的分隔符號和語彙基元，類似於路由和 C# 語言所使用的分隔符號和語彙基元。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-901">Regular expressions use delimiters and tokens similar to those used by Routing and the C# language.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-902">規則運算式的語彙基元必須逸出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-902">Regular expression tokens must be escaped.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-903">若要在路由中使用規則運算式 `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$`，運算式必須以字串中所提供的 `\` (單一反斜線) 字元作為 C# 原始程式檔中的 `\\` (雙反斜線) 字元，才能逸出 `\` 字串逸出字元 (除非使用[逐字字串常值](/dotnet/csharp/language-reference/keywords/string))。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-903">To use the regular expression `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` in routing, the expression must have the `\` (single backslash) characters provided in the string as `\\` (double backslash) characters in the C# source file in order to escape the `\` string escape character (unless using [verbatim string literals](/dotnet/csharp/language-reference/keywords/string)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-904">若要逸出路由參數分隔符號字元 (`{`、`}`、`[`、`]`)，請在運算式中使用雙字元 (`{{`、`}`、`[[`、`]]`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-904">To escape routing parameter delimiter characters (`{`, `}`, `[`, `]`), double the characters in the expression (`{{`, `}`, `[[`, `]]`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-905">下表顯示規則運算式和逸出的版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-905">The following table shows a regular expression and the escaped version.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-906">規則運算式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-906">Regular Expression</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-907">逸出的規則運算式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-907">Escaped Regular Expression</span></span>     |
| --------------------- | ------------------------------ |
| `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` | `^\\d{{3}}-\\d{{2}}-\\d{{4}}$` |
| `^[a-z]{2}$`          | `^[[a-z]]{{2}}$`               |

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-908">路由中所使用的規則運算式通常以插入號 (`^`) 字元開頭，並符合字串的開始位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-908">Regular expressions used in routing often start with the caret (`^`) character and match starting position of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-909">運算式通常以貨幣符號 (`$`) 字元結尾，並符合字串的結尾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-909">The expressions often end with the dollar sign (`$`) character and match end of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-910">`^` 和 `$` 字元可確保規則運算式符合整個路由參數值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-910">The `^` and `$` characters ensure that the regular expression match the entire route parameter value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-911">若不使用 `^` 與 `$` 字元，規則運算式會比對字串內的所有部分字串，這通常不是您想要的結果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-911">Without the `^` and `$` characters, the regular expression match any substring within the string, which is often undesirable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-912">下表提供範例，並說明它們符合或無法符合的原因。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-912">The following table provides examples and explains why they match or fail to match.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-913">運算式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-913">Expression</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-914">字串</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-914">String</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-915">比對</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-915">Match</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-916">註解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-916">Comment</span></span>               |
| ------------ | --------- | :---: |  -------------------- |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-917">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-917">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-918">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-918">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-919">子字串相符項目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-919">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-920">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-920">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-921">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-921">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-922">子字串相符項目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-922">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-923">mz</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-923">mz</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-924">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-924">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-925">符合運算式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-925">Matches expression</span></span>    |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-926">MZ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-926">MZ</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-927">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-927">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-928">不區分大小寫</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-928">Not case sensitive</span></span>    |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-929">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-929">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-930">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-930">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-931">請參閱上述的 `^` 和 `$`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-931">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-932">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-932">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-933">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-933">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-934">請參閱上述的 `^` 和 `$`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-934">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-935">如需規則運算式語法的詳細資訊，請參閱 [.NET Framework 規則運算式](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-935">For more information on regular expression syntax, see [.NET Framework Regular Expressions](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-936">若要將參數限制為一組已知的可能值，請使用規則運算式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-936">To constrain a parameter to a known set of possible values, use a regular expression.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-937">例如，`{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}` 只會將 `action` 路由值與 `list`、`get` 或 `create` 相符。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-937">For example, `{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}` only matches the `action` route value to `list`, `get`, or `create`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-938">如果已傳入條件約束字典，字串 `^(list|get|create)$` 則是對等項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-938">If passed into the constraints dictionary, the string `^(list|get|create)$` is equivalent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-939">已傳入條件約束字典 (未內嵌在範本內) 的條件約束，即使不符合其中一個已知的條件約束，也會被視為規則運算式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-939">Constraints that are passed in the constraints dictionary (not inline within a template) that don't match one of the known constraints are also treated as regular expressions.</span></span>

## <a name="custom-route-constraints"></a><span data-ttu-id="f01e9-940">自訂路由限制式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-940">Custom Route Constraints</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-941">除了內建的路由限制式之外，自訂路由限制式也可以透過實作 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> 介面來建立。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-941">In addition to the built-in route constraints, custom route constraints can be created by implementing the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> interface.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-942"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> 介面包含單一方法 `Match`，此方法會在滿足限制式時傳回 `true`，否則會傳回 `false`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-942">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> interface contains a single method, `Match`, which returns `true` if the constraint is satisfied and `false` otherwise.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-943">若要使用自訂 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>，路由限制式型別必須必須向應用程式的 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> (在應用程式的服務容器中) 註冊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-943">To use a custom <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>, the route constraint type must be registered with the app's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> in the app's service container.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-944"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> 是一個目錄，它將路由限制式機碼對應到可驗證那些限制式的 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> 實作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-944">A <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> is a dictionary that maps route constraint keys to <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> implementations that validate those constraints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-945">更新應用程式的 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> 時，可在 `Startup.ConfigureServices` 中於進行 [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) 呼叫時更新，或透過使用 `services.Configure<RouteOptions>` 直接設定 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions> 來更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-945">An app's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> can be updated in `Startup.ConfigureServices` either as part of a [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) call or by configuring <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions> directly with `services.Configure<RouteOptions>`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-946">例如：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-946">For example:</span></span>

```csharp
services.AddRouting(options =>
{
    options.ConstraintMap.Add("customName", typeof(MyCustomConstraint));
});
```

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-947">限制式接著能以一般方式套用到路由 (使用註冊限制式型別時使用名稱)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-947">The constraint can then be applied to routes in the usual manner, using the name specified when registering the constraint type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-948">例如：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-948">For example:</span></span>

```csharp
[HttpGet("{id:customName}")]
public ActionResult<string> Get(string id)
```

## <a name="parameter-transformer-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="f01e9-949">參數轉換器參考</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-949">Parameter transformer reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-950">參數轉換程式：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-950">Parameter transformers:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-951">會在為 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> 產生連結時執行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-951">Execute when generating a link for a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-952">實作 `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IOutboundParameterTransformer`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-952">Implement `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IOutboundParameterTransformer`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-953">是使用 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> 進行設定的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-953">Are configured using <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-954">採用參數的路由值，並將它轉換為新的字串值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-954">Take the parameter's route value and transform it to a new string value.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-955">導致在所產生連結中使用已轉換的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-955">Result in using the transformed value in the generated link.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-956">例如，具有 `Url.Action(new { article = "MyTestArticle" })` 之路由模式 `blog\{article:slugify}` 中的自訂 `slugify` 參數轉換器，會產生 `blog\my-test-article`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-956">For example, a custom `slugify` parameter transformer in route pattern `blog\{article:slugify}` with `Url.Action(new { article = "MyTestArticle" })` generates `blog\my-test-article`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-957">若要在路由模式中使用參數轉換器，請先在 `Startup.ConfigureServices` 中使用 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> 進行設定：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-957">To use a parameter transformer in a route pattern, configure it first using <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> in `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span></span>

```csharp
services.AddRouting(options =>
{
    // Replace the type and the name used to refer to it with your own
    // IOutboundParameterTransformer implementation
    options.ConstraintMap["slugify"] = typeof(SlugifyParameterTransformer);
});
```

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-958">架構會使用參數轉換器來轉換端點解析的 URI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-958">Parameter transformers are used by the framework to transform the URI where an endpoint resolves.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-959">例如，ASP.NET Core MVC 會使用參數轉換器，轉換用於比對 `area`、`controller`、`action` 和 `page` 的路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-959">For example, ASP.NET Core MVC uses parameter transformers to transform the route value used to match an `area`, `controller`, `action`, and `page`.</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller:slugify=Home}/{action:slugify=Index}/{id?}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-960">使用上述的路由，動作 `SubscriptionManagementController.GetAll()` 會與URI `/subscription-management/get-all` 比對。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-960">With the preceding route, the action `SubscriptionManagementController.GetAll()` is matched with the URI `/subscription-management/get-all`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-961">參數轉換器不會變更用來產生連結的路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-961">A parameter transformer doesn't change the route values used to generate a link.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-962">例如，`Url.Action("GetAll", "SubscriptionManagement")` 會輸出 `/subscription-management/get-all`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-962">For example, `Url.Action("GetAll", "SubscriptionManagement")` outputs `/subscription-management/get-all`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-963">ASP.NET Core 針對搭配產生的路由使用參數轉換程式提供了 API 慣例：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-963">ASP.NET Core provides API conventions for using a parameter transformers with generated routes:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-964">ASP.NET Core MVC 有 `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.RouteTokenTransformerConvention` API 慣例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-964">ASP.NET Core MVC has the `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.RouteTokenTransformerConvention` API convention.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-965">此慣例會將所指定參數轉換程式套用到應用程式中的所有屬性路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-965">This convention applies a specified parameter transformer to all attribute routes in the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-966">參數轉換程式會在被取代時轉換屬性路由語彙基元。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-966">The parameter transformer transforms attribute route tokens as they are replaced.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-967">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[使用參數轉換程式自訂語彙基元取代](/aspnet/core/mvc/controllers/routing#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-token-replacement)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-967">For more information, see [Use a parameter transformer to customize token replacement](/aspnet/core/mvc/controllers/routing#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-token-replacement).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-968">Razor Pages 有 `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.PageRouteTransformerConvention` API 慣例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-968">Razor Pages has the `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.PageRouteTransformerConvention` API convention.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-969">此慣例會將所指定參數轉換器套用至所有自動探索到的 Razor Pages。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-969">This convention applies a specified parameter transformer to all automatically discovered Razor Pages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-970">參數轉換器會轉換 Razor Pages 路由的資料夾與檔案名稱區段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-970">The parameter transformer transforms the folder and file name segments of Razor Pages routes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-971">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[使用參數轉換程式自訂頁面路由](/aspnet/core/razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-page-routes)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-971">For more information, see [Use a parameter transformer to customize page routes](/aspnet/core/razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-page-routes).</span></span>

## <a name="url-generation-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="f01e9-972">URL 產生參考</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-972">URL generation reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-973">下列範例示範如何在指定路由值字典和 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteCollection> 的情況下產生路由的連結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-973">The following example shows how to generate a link to a route given a dictionary of route values and a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteCollection>.</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/2.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_Dictionary)]

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-974">在上述範例的結尾產生的 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath> 是 `/package/create/123`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-974">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath> generated at the end of the preceding sample is `/package/create/123`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-975">字典提供「追蹤套件路由」範本 `package/{operation}/{id}` 的 `operation` 和 `id` 路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-975">The dictionary supplies the `operation` and `id` route values of the "Track Package Route" template, `package/{operation}/{id}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-976">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[使用路由中介軟體](#use-routing-middleware)一節或[範例應用程式](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples)中的範例程式碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-976">For details, see the sample code in the [Use Routing Middleware](#use-routing-middleware) section or the [sample app](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-977"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext> 建構函式的第二個參數是「環境值」的集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-977">The second parameter to the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext> constructor is a collection of *ambient values*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-978">環境值便於使用，因為它們會限制開發人員必須在要求內容中指定的值數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-978">Ambient values are convenient to use because they limit the number of values a developer must specify within a request context.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-979">目前要求的目前路由值被視為用於連結產生的環境值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-979">The current route values of the current request are considered ambient values for link generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-980">在 ASP.NET Core MVC 應用程式 `HomeController` 的 `About` 動作中，您不需要指定控制器路由值以連結到 `Index` 動作&mdash;會使用 `Home` 的環境值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-980">In an ASP.NET Core MVC app's `About` action of the `HomeController`, you don't need to specify the controller route value to link to the `Index` action&mdash;the ambient value of `Home` is used.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-981">不符合參數的環境值會予以忽略。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-981">Ambient values that don't match a parameter are ignored.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-982">當明確提供的值覆寫環境值時，也會忽略環境值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-982">Ambient values are also ignored when an explicitly provided value overrides the ambient value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-983">URL 中的比對是從左到右。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-983">Matching occurs from left to right in the URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-984">明確提供但不符合路由區段的值會新增至查詢字串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-984">Values explicitly provided but that don't match a segment of the route are added to the query string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-985">下表顯示使用路由範本 `{controller}/{action}/{id?}` 時的結果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-985">The following table shows the result when using the route template `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-986">環境值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-986">Ambient Values</span></span>                     | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-987">明確值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-987">Explicit Values</span></span>                        | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-988">結果</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-988">Result</span></span>                  |
| ---------------------------------- | -------------------------------------- | ----------------------- |
| <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-989">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-989">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-990">action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-990">action = "About"</span></span>                       | `/Home/About`           |
| <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-991">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-991">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-992">controller = "Order", action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-992">controller = "Order", action = "About"</span></span> | `/Order/About`          |
| <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-993">controller = "Home", color = "Red"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-993">controller = "Home", color = "Red"</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-994">action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-994">action = "About"</span></span>                       | `/Home/About`           |
| <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-995">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-995">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-996">action = "About", color = "Red"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-996">action = "About", color = "Red"</span></span>        | `/Home/About?color=Red` |

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-997">如果路由具有未對應至參數的預設值，且該值會明確提供，它必須符合預設值：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-997">If a route has a default value that doesn't correspond to a parameter and that value is explicitly provided, it must match the default value:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute("blog_route", "blog/{*slug}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Blog", action = "ReadPost" });
```
