| `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` | `^\\d{{3}}-\\d{{2}}-\\d{{4}}$` |
| `^[a-z]{2}$`          | `^[[a-z]]{{2}}$`               |

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1280">路由中所使用的規則運算式通常以插入號 (`^`) 字元開頭，並符合字串的開始位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1280">Regular expressions used in routing often start with the caret (`^`) character and match starting position of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1281">運算式通常以貨幣符號 (`$`) 字元結尾，並符合字串的結尾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1281">The expressions often end with the dollar sign (`$`) character and match end of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1282">`^` 和 `$` 字元可確保規則運算式符合整個路由參數值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1282">The `^` and `$` characters ensure that the regular expression match the entire route parameter value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1283">若不使用 `^` 與 `$` 字元，規則運算式會比對字串內的所有部分字串，這通常不是您想要的結果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1283">Without the `^` and `$` characters, the regular expression match any substring within the string, which is often undesirable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1284">下表提供範例，並說明它們符合或無法符合的原因。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1284">The following table provides examples and explains why they match or fail to match.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1285">運算式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1285">Expression</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1286">字串</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1286">String</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1287">比對</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1287">Match</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1288">註解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1288">Comment</span></span>               |
| ------------ | --------- | :---: |  -------------------- |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1289">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1289">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1290">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1290">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1291">子字串相符項目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1291">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1292">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1292">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1293">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1293">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1294">子字串相符項目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1294">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1295">mz</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1295">mz</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1296">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1296">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1297">符合運算式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1297">Matches expression</span></span>    |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1298">MZ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1298">MZ</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1299">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1299">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1300">不區分大小寫</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1300">Not case sensitive</span></span>    |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1301">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1301">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1302">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1302">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1303">請參閱上述的 `^` 和 `$`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1303">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1304">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1304">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1305">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1305">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1306">請參閱上述的 `^` 和 `$`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1306">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1307">如需規則運算式語法的詳細資訊，請參閱 [.NET Framework 規則運算式](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1307">For more information on regular expression syntax, see [.NET Framework Regular Expressions](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1308">若要將參數限制為一組已知的可能值，請使用規則運算式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1308">To constrain a parameter to a known set of possible values, use a regular expression.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1309">例如，`{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}` 只會將 `action` 路由值與 `list`、`get` 或 `create` 相符。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1309">For example, `{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}` only matches the `action` route value to `list`, `get`, or `create`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1310">如果已傳入條件約束字典，字串 `^(list|get|create)$` 則是對等項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1310">If passed into the constraints dictionary, the string `^(list|get|create)$` is equivalent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1311">已傳入條件約束字典 (未內嵌在範本內) 的條件約束，即使不符合其中一個已知的條件約束，也會被視為規則運算式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1311">Constraints that are passed in the constraints dictionary (not inline within a template) that don't match one of the known constraints are also treated as regular expressions.</span></span>

## <a name="custom-route-constraints"></a><span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1312">自訂路由限制式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1312">Custom Route Constraints</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1313">除了內建的路由限制式之外，自訂路由限制式也可以透過實作 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> 介面來建立。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1313">In addition to the built-in route constraints, custom route constraints can be created by implementing the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> interface.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1314"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> 介面包含單一方法 `Match`，此方法會在滿足限制式時傳回 `true`，否則會傳回 `false`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1314">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> interface contains a single method, `Match`, which returns `true` if the constraint is satisfied and `false` otherwise.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1315">若要使用自訂 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>，路由限制式型別必須必須向應用程式的 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> (在應用程式的服務容器中) 註冊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1315">To use a custom <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>, the route constraint type must be registered with the app's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> in the app's service container.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1316"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> 是一個目錄，它將路由限制式機碼對應到可驗證那些限制式的 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> 實作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1316">A <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> is a dictionary that maps route constraint keys to <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> implementations that validate those constraints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1317">更新應用程式的 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> 時，可在 `Startup.ConfigureServices` 中於進行 [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) 呼叫時更新，或透過使用 `services.Configure<RouteOptions>` 直接設定 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions> 來更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1317">An app's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> can be updated in `Startup.ConfigureServices` either as part of a [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) call or by configuring <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions> directly with `services.Configure<RouteOptions>`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1318">例如：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1318">For example:</span></span>

```csharp
services.AddRouting(options =>
{
    options.ConstraintMap.Add("customName", typeof(MyCustomConstraint));
});
```

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1319">限制式接著能以一般方式套用到路由 (使用註冊限制式型別時使用名稱)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1319">The constraint can then be applied to routes in the usual manner, using the name specified when registering the constraint type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1320">例如：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1320">For example:</span></span>

```csharp
[HttpGet("{id:customName}")]
public ActionResult<string> Get(string id)
```

## <a name="url-generation-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1321">URL 產生參考</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1321">URL generation reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1322">下列範例示範如何在指定路由值字典和 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteCollection> 的情況下產生路由的連結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1322">The following example shows how to generate a link to a route given a dictionary of route values and a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteCollection>.</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/2.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_Dictionary)]

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1323">在上述範例的結尾產生的 <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath> 是 `/package/create/123`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1323">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath> generated at the end of the preceding sample is `/package/create/123`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1324">字典提供「追蹤套件路由」範本 `package/{operation}/{id}` 的 `operation` 和 `id` 路由值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1324">The dictionary supplies the `operation` and `id` route values of the "Track Package Route" template, `package/{operation}/{id}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1325">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[使用路由中介軟體](#use-routing-middleware)一節或[範例應用程式](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples)中的範例程式碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1325">For details, see the sample code in the [Use Routing Middleware](#use-routing-middleware) section or the [sample app](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1326"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext> 建構函式的第二個參數是「環境值」的集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1326">The second parameter to the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext> constructor is a collection of *ambient values*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1327">環境值便於使用，因為它們會限制開發人員必須在要求內容中指定的值數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1327">Ambient values are convenient to use because they limit the number of values a developer must specify within a request context.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1328">目前要求的目前路由值被視為用於連結產生的環境值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1328">The current route values of the current request are considered ambient values for link generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1329">在 ASP.NET Core MVC 應用程式 `HomeController` 的 `About` 動作中，您不需要指定控制器路由值以連結到 `Index` 動作&mdash;會使用 `Home` 的環境值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1329">In an ASP.NET Core MVC app's `About` action of the `HomeController`, you don't need to specify the controller route value to link to the `Index` action&mdash;the ambient value of `Home` is used.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1330">不符合參數的環境值會予以忽略。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1330">Ambient values that don't match a parameter are ignored.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1331">當明確提供的值覆寫環境值時，也會忽略環境值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1331">Ambient values are also ignored when an explicitly provided value overrides the ambient value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1332">URL 中的比對是從左到右。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1332">Matching occurs from left to right in the URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1333">明確提供但不符合路由區段的值會新增至查詢字串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1333">Values explicitly provided but that don't match a segment of the route are added to the query string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1334">下表顯示使用路由範本 `{controller}/{action}/{id?}` 時的結果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1334">The following table shows the result when using the route template `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1335">環境值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1335">Ambient Values</span></span>                     | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1336">明確值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1336">Explicit Values</span></span>                        | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1337">結果</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1337">Result</span></span>                  |
| ---------------------------------- | -------------------------------------- | ----------------------- |
| <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1338">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1338">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1339">action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1339">action = "About"</span></span>                       | `/Home/About`           |
| <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1340">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1340">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1341">controller = "Order", action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1341">controller = "Order", action = "About"</span></span> | `/Order/About`          |
| <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1342">controller = "Home", color = "Red"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1342">controller = "Home", color = "Red"</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1343">action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1343">action = "About"</span></span>                       | `/Home/About`           |
| <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1344">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1344">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1345">action = "About", color = "Red"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1345">action = "About", color = "Red"</span></span>        | `/Home/About?color=Red` |

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1346">如果路由具有未對應至參數的預設值，且該值會明確提供，它必須符合預設值：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1346">If a route has a default value that doesn't correspond to a parameter and that value is explicitly provided, it must match the default value:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute("blog_route", "blog/{*slug}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Blog", action = "ReadPost" });
```

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1347">連結產生只有在提供了 `controller` 與 `action` 的相符值時，才會產生此路由的連結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1347">Link generation only generates a link for this route when the matching values for `controller` and `action` are provided.</span></span>

## <a name="complex-segments"></a><span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1348">複雜區段</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1348">Complex segments</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1349">複雜區段 (例如，`[Route("/x{token}y")]`) 會透過以非窮盡的方式，由右至左比對常值來處理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1349">Complex segments (for example `[Route("/x{token}y")]`) are processed by matching up literals from right to left in a non-greedy way.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1350">請參閱[此程式碼](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293)以了解如何比對複雜區段的詳細解釋。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1350">See [this code](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) for a detailed explanation of how complex segments are matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f01e9-1351">[程式法範例](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293)不是由 ASP.NET Core 使用，但它提供一個好的複雜區段解釋。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f01e9-1351">The [code sample](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) is not used by ASP.NET Core, but it provides a good explanation of complex segments.</span></span>
